French Naval Minister Explains - The Process of Concluding the Naval Treaty

(Paris) Naval Minister Pietri recently gave an interview to a reporter from "L'Intransigeant," commenting on the naval treaty signed by Britain, France, and the United States on March 25. He said, "According to this treaty, the tonnage of various types of ships has been clearly stipulated, and the signatory countries will not compete with each other in terms of tonnage and can be in an equal position. However, the naval needs of each signatory country can still be freely estimated and have not been restricted. The long-term constraints previously accepted by the French Navy (referring to the ratio system stipulated by the Washington Naval Treaty) have now been lifted. According to the Washington Naval Treaty, the strength stipulated for the French Navy was one-third of the British and American navies, or slightly more than one-half of the Japanese navy, and it was on par with the Italian navy. Although France was happy to accept the obligations of this treaty, it was limited to battleships, and it was unwilling to accept the same restriction method for various auxiliary ships at that time. Therefore, France refused to sign the 1930 London Naval Treaty in order to restore its strength before the European War. The newly concluded treaty has now canceled the ratio system stipulated by the Washington Naval Treaty. This is due to Japan's opposition, and France has also consistently refused to extend it. We have frankly stated this view to British First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell in July 1934 when Britain invited the relevant countries to hold preliminary naval conference talks. In short, our goal is to obtain freedom. Japan's purpose in withdrawing shortly after the opening of the naval conference is different from ours, not satisfied with obtaining freedom, but wants to require Britain and the United States to reduce their existing naval forces in order to realize equal rights, which Britain and the United States are unwilling to do and therefore resolutely rejected. Pietri then said that although Japan and Italy both refused to participate in the new naval treaty, their views are completely different. It is currently impossible to know what attitude Japan will adopt in the future. Therefore, it is necessary to stipulate protective clauses in the new naval treaty (these clauses stipulate that if the shipbuilding programs of non-signatory countries exceed the provisions of the naval treaty, the signatory countries can restore their freedom). As for Italy, its views on the new naval treaty are the same as those of Britain, France, and the United States. The reason why it refuses to sign is purely due to political factors. Italy has expressed approval of the new naval treaty in general and has never opposed it. There is no doubt that it will be able to respect it in the future. As for Germany, although it is not a signatory to the new naval treaty, if its shipbuilding program exceeds the provisions in the future, the protective clauses should be implemented. I think it is appropriate for Germany to participate in the new naval treaty. Germany should do so, and so should Soviet Russia, because the Soviet Navy has not accepted any restrictive measures to date. Regarding this level, the relevant countries have not yet determined what procedures should be adopted. Previously, when the naval conference was held, the British representative originally advocated inviting Germany and Russia to attend and participate. At that time, the French representative believed that the naval conference should only be attended by representatives of the signatory countries to the Washington Naval Treaty, and he rejected the British proposal. France proposed two methods: 1. The signatory countries to the Washington Naval Treaty should first establish a treaty; 2. Then, other countries should sign and participate, hoping to establish a general agreement. General negotiations could have started at that time, but because the United States did not feel interested in this, it advocated that the signatory countries to the Washington Naval Treaty should continue negotiations in order to speed up the naval conference. Therefore, the new treaty was only signed by Britain, the United States, and France, and Britain conducted separate negotiations with other countries to complete a general agreement. But I don't know whether the current international situation will facilitate the implementation of this plan. As for the mutual notification of shipbuilding programs, what France advocates is that "although countries can build ships freely, they must clearly announce it." The French political system is parliamentary, and any secret action is not allowed. What is worrying is that other countries deliberately play tricks or even adopt lightning-fast means. In addition, the various qualitative restrictions stipulated in the new naval treaty do not hinder French naval policy. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

Hurricane Disaster in America

Houses Blown Down, Numerous Deaths and Injuries. Churches Temporarily Converted into Funeral Homes

Tupelo, Mississippi, USA. A major storm swept through Tupelo, Mississippi today. The death toll is between 100 and 125, and hundreds are injured. Many houses were blown down, including a hospital, and several buildings were blown into the lake. The black residential area was completely destroyed. The governor has mobilized the National Guard to maintain order. Churches have been converted into funeral homes, and hospitals are filled with the dead and injured. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Motor Vessel Tricolor Suffers Mishap. Passengers Safe and Sound

San Francisco. The Norwegian motor vessel Tricolor (6,850 tons) was en route from Manila via Hong Kong, Shanghai, and various Japanese ports to San Francisco when it suffered a mishap about a thousand miles from Yokohama. All passengers on board were safely transferred to an American vessel, including two American women who boarded in Shanghai. The Tricolor belongs to the Wilhelmsen Barber Steamship Company, and Tientsin Yang Hing is its agent in Shanghai. There were a total of sixteen passengers on board, with forty crew members, including six women and five children. Seven of them boarded in Manila, and the remaining four boarded in Hong Kong. After the ship's mishap, it sent out a distress signal, which was received by several ships. The closest one was the Socony-Vacuum Oil Company's oil tanker Yarrowdale (8,627 tons), which was en route from Dalian to California. The two ships communicated by radio and sailed towards each other at full speed. Initially, due to the darkness of the night and rough seas, the passengers could not be transferred, but eventually all were rescued. Relatives of the Manila passengers were initially worried upon hearing the news of the ship's mishap. Last night, an American resident received a telegram from his mother on board, stating that everyone was safe, which greatly comforted everyone. According to the Yarrowdale's report, the Tricolor is now trying to run aground on a shoal in Honolulu or Yokohama. The fire on board is still dangerous, but it has not spread. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Bank of Japan Reduces Discount Rate

(Tokyo) The Bank of Japan held a board meeting at 2 p.m. on the 6th and decided to reduce the legal discount interest rate by 1%, effective from the 7th. The bank authorities announced the details at 5:20 p.m. as follows: Discount rate for commercial paper: 9 rin per 100 yen per day (current rate: 1 sen per day). Interest rate on loans secured by government bonds and discount rate on notes guaranteed by government bonds: 1 sen or more per 100 yen per day (current rate: 1 sen 1 rin or more per day). Interest rate on loans secured by items other than government bonds and discount rate on notes guaranteed by items other than government bonds: 1 sen 1 rin or more per 100 yen per day (current rate: 1 sen 2 rin or more per day). Overdraft interest rate: 1 sen 3 rin per 100 yen per day (current rate: 1 sen 4 rin per day) (6th Dometsu Dispatch)

Present State of Shenyang Industry Due to Japanese Initiative: Once the Origin of the Incident, Now a Japanese Industrial Zone

Shenyang, the origin of the September 18th Incident, has now become a Japanese industrial zone. Various light and heavy industries such as enamel, iron, hardware, wool weaving, hemp manufacturing, winemaking, tobacco, and soy sauce brewing are all available. The active initiative of the Japanese is evident. The various industrial conditions are recorded as follows:

Tobacco: The sales volume (quantity) of the Dongya Tobacco Shenyang Factory increased by 15% last month. Compared to the same period last year, it has almost increased by 40%. Also, due to the implementation of taxation by the puppet organization, the Dongya Tobacco "Golden Gun" brand required in Shenyang, concerning tax matters, prior contracts were made and many were concluded.

Hardware: This year, companies worried about overproduction from last year and restricted production. Overall, sales this year can be considered good. The Shenyang hardware industry had a stock of 8 million yuan in March, all of which were absorbed. Approximately 15 million pieces were contracted with the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) and others. "Manzhou" hardware has already contracted half of its six-month production. The market price is 9 rin.

Hemp Manufacturing: The production volume of Shenyang hemp manufacturing is not much different from the previous month, about 500,000 pieces. The company's factory in the Yingkou affiliated area is full of products. Most of the factory's products are transported to North Manchuria.

Wool Weaving: The production volume of Man-Mongol wool weaving is unchanged from the previous month, reaching 100,000 (270,000) pieces. Sales volume is approximately 330,000 yuan, an increase of 20% from the previous month. The puppet public office has approved 30% fewer new batches for the new year, but there is a large demand for wool fabrics from civilians, and sales in Shanghai and North China are gradually becoming active. Currently, the shipping of Western-style clothing fabrics to North Manchuria in April is not active, but it is better than before. The market price is weak at 24 sen and 2 rin.

Ironworks: The Dalian Machinery Shenyang Factory has no new contracts, and the production volume is 2 million. It is spending its time in a leisurely manner. Due to the ice-free period for Japanese "Man" steel materials, handling in March was already active.

Brewing: All factories producing sake, soy sauce, and sorghum liquor are ordinary. (Tohoku News Agency)

Hong Kong Court: Second Trial Regarding the Wang Jingwei Assassination Case: Only Testimony Regarding the Events from Witnesses from Nanjing; Wang Yaqiao Boasts Himself as the "King of Assassins"

Hong Kong Correspondence. After the Hong Kong government arrested Yu Likui (also known as Li Zi'an and Li Shiru), Zhou Shiping, Hu Dahai, and Zhang Zhihan, the key suspects in the Wang Jingwei assassination case, the Nanjing government sent a letter to Hong Kong requesting their extradition for prosecution. The case was officially heard by Judge Shi of the Central Tribunal on the 30th, and a continued hearing was held at 2:30 p.m. on the 1st. After the court was convened, Li Zhizheng, the deputy investigator of the Nanjing Police Department, was first called to the witness stand. He testified, "Hu Yunqing was the president of the Nanjing Chenguang News Agency, also known as Hua Kezhi. He Po Guang was the editor of the agency, located at 2 Huanghelou Street, Nanjing. When I searched the agency, I found completed printed manuscripts. I also discovered a letter, which is currently kept by the Nanjing Police Department. The letter stated that the assassination of Wang Jingwei was our doing and had nothing to do with Guo Yongmou. The letter was addressed to the gentlemen for their perusal. In addition, there was a pile of scrap paper with printed text, resembling a news draft, stating that Wang Jingwei had been assassinated. Zhang Yuhua was arrested in Shanghai on November 16th. He Po Guang was arrested in Zhenjiang on November 3rd last year. Gu Zifeng and his wife, as well as Sun Fengming's wife, were also arrested at the same time. All those arrested gave confessions. According to Nanjing's publication regulations, all news agencies must register their address and staff. The registration date for Chenguang News Agency was September 26, 1934. The applicant for registration was Hu Yunqing, the address was 2 Huanghelou Street, and the registered editor was He Po Guang. There were a total of four registered reporters, including the deceased Sun Fengming."

At this point, the defendant's lawyer, Xi Bingxi, stood up to question him. Li replied, "I saw Sun Fengming at the Central Hospital. Sun's injuries were also very severe. He was suffering from gunshot wounds. He was more conscious than Wang at the time. The ward was not full of visitors. Besides myself, there were two other people, and there were two police officers guarding outside the room. Although the assassination case was serious, I was ordered to investigate the matter and therefore had the right to handle it. I visited Sun Yiming for half an hour. Sun died at midnight on November 2nd. Before the assassination occurred, I had never met Sun Fengming. After the incident, I was ordered to search the agency. By then, everyone in the agency had already fled. The situation inside the agency was extremely chaotic. I searched everywhere and only found a large pile of ashes in the kitchen. There were very few documents in the agency. There were also remnants of burned paper in the pile of ashes, stating that Wang Jingwei had been assassinated."

After Li Zhi finished testifying, the judge ordered him to sign the deposition and step down. Next, Wang Renshan (also known as Wang Baishi), another witness from the Nanjing government, testified. He stated, "I was born in Qiongzhou. At the age of seven, I entered elementary school in Guangzhou. At that time, my father worked in Chinese politics. In 1921, at the age of fifteen, I transferred to Nanjing to study. After graduating from middle school, I transferred to Peking University. In 1928, at the age of 23, I dropped out of school and worked at the Nanjing Kuomintang Central Party Headquarters for about three or four months. Later, I returned to Guangzhou and worked at the Guangdong Provincial Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang. Since 1930, I have been unemployed and have resided in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Hong Kong. All expenses were provided by my father, who was the secretary of the Qiongyai Chamber of Commerce. I also returned to my hometown of Qiongyai. In 1923, when I was seventeen, I met Wang Yaqiao in Shanghai. I became friends with him. At that time, he was unemployed at home. Later, when I worked in Nanjing, I often met with him. I also knew Chen Huixi. In Hong Kong, he led me to Wang Yaqiao's house on Wanzai Road. Wang's friend was named Mai Kongzhang. In 1934, I met the first defendant, Yu Likui. I also visited Wang Yaqiao. At that time, Yu Likui was also known as Li Zi'an and lived in a building on Yongxing Street. I visited him according to the address. Our relationship was quite harmonious. At that time, Wang Yaqiao and Yu Likui, etc., had no legitimate occupation. Wang Yaqiao trusted me very much. He often boasted to me that he was a 'King of Assassins' and had single-handedly carried out many assassination cases in Shanghai. Even the first defendant, Yu Likui, had heard him boast in this way. He also said that his most proud 'masterpiece' was the assassination attempt on Song Ziwen at the North Railway Station in Shanghai, because he was able to carry out the assassination under the noses of the military police and get away safely, which was why he was so proud of himself. At that time, they were planning the assassination in Hong Kong. I heard that someone had offered a large reward for the assassination of Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei, but I do not know who offered the reward. At that time, the defendants Zhou Shiping and Hu Dahai lived with Yu Likui and resided in a building on Yongxing Street. When Wang Yaqiao talked to me about the assassination of Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei, the defendants Zhou Shiping and Hu Dahai were present. I met Hua Kezhi in July 1934 at Wang Yaqiao's house in Wanzai. He was staying at Wang Yaqiao's house. After Hua arrived in Hong Kong, he held several meetings. Those present included Wang Yaqiao, Hua Kezhi, Yu Likui, Zhou Shiping, Hu Dahai, and myself. The content of the discussions was about carrying out the assassination of Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei. It was decided to establish a news agency in Nanjing. This proposal was put forward by Wang Yaqiao. The name of the agency was Chenguang, and Zhang Yuhua was appointed as the general manager. Zhang was a former subordinate of Wang Yaqiao and Yu Likui. He Po Guang was appointed as the editor-in-chief, Gu Zifeng was appointed as the general affairs, and Sun Fengming, Liu Shurong, and others were appointed as reporters. The purpose of setting up the news agency was nothing more than to take advantage of the superior position of news reporters, who could approach general party and government officials and seize opportunities to act. At that time, they advocated appointing Sun Fengming as a reporter and also recommended the third defendant, Hu Dahai. When Hu heard this, he expressed his willingness to go. As for the agency's source of funding and the monthly allowance, I do not know anything about it. After this matter was decided, Hua Kezhi left Hong Kong in July and returned to Hong Kong once in September," and so on. By this point, it was already past 5 o'clock, and the judge ordered that the defendants be remanded in custody and await further trial at a later date. It is reported that in addition to sending several police officers and witnesses to Hong Kong to testify, Nanjing is now sending another seven or eight witnesses to Hong Kong to testify. These seven or eight people will arrive in Hong Kong successively during the day. This reporter visited Xi Bingxi, the defense lawyer for the defendants in this case, to inquire about the handling of the case. According to him, the Nanjing side attaches great importance to this case, and the case has become serious. Therefore, it will take three to several months to conclude the case. (2nd)

Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea: Establishment of a Transportation and Sales Committee, Active Improvement of Transportation and Sales Methods, and Encouragement of Tea Firms to Manufacture Tea

Anqing Dispatch: The Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea Transportation and Sales Committee held its inaugural meeting in Anqing on April 1st. The Agricultural Department of the National Economic Council, the Jiangxi Provincial Government, and both the Finance and Construction Departments sent representatives to attend. Yang Mianzhong, Director of the Anhui Provincial Finance Department, Liu Yiyan, Director of the Construction Department, as well as tea industry experts and bank representatives, also attended. The meeting lasted for three days, and resolved to organize general and branch transportation and sales offices, unify transportation and sales, raise funds to loan to tea firms, and improve tea manufacturing, among other important matters. Upon visiting the committee, Permanent Committee Member and Director of the Anhui Provincial Construction Department, Liu Yiyan, provided the following detailed information:

"The black teas of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces are traditionally divided into three types: Qihong, Ninghong, and Hehong. Qihong is produced in Qimen, Zhide in Anhui, and Fuliang in Jiangxi, three counties; Ninghong is produced in Xiushui, Tonggu, and Wuning in Jiangxi, three counties; and Hehong is produced in Qianshan and other counties in Jiangxi. They have long enjoyed a high reputation in the international market, with annual exports reaching over 500,000 cases at their peak. In recent years, the situation has steadily declined. Qihong's annual production is now 60,000 cases, Ninghong only 10,000 cases, and Hehong has completely disappeared. The reasons for this are partly due to the rise of teas from India, Ceylon, Java, and Japan, which have seized our markets. However, it is also due to the weak financial resources and lack of organization of tea farmers and tea firms, which allows intermediate merchants to manipulate and exploit them, leading to a complete collapse. The prominent drawbacks include increased costs, susceptibility to unexpected losses, confusion of product prices, and the instigation of speculation. Anhui Province originally had a tea improvement farm in Qimen, which was jointly operated with the Industrial Department of the National Economic Council two years ago, increasing funding and fully equipping it to improve planting and manufacturing. In February of this year, the National Economic Council convened a tea technology discussion meeting. The Anhui Construction Department proposed the establishment of a Qihong Transportation and Sales Committee to use tea firms' loan proceeds to collect tea to benefit the specialty product. This was approved in principle. After the meeting, the Anhui Provincial Government sent personnel to consult with Jiangxi Province and obtained their agreement to expand the scope of assistance to include both Qihong and Ninghong, organizing the Anhui-Jiangxi Black Tea Transportation and Sales Committee. Now that the committee has been established, the implementation measures are as follows: After registering tea firms, loans will be processed. Whether providing direct loans or introducing loans, efforts will be made to reduce interest rates. In terms of transportation, the highways and railways of both provinces will be used to reduce freight costs and ensure fast and safe transportation. In terms of sales, experts from China and abroad will be invited to evaluate the prices, so that consumers are not deceived and producers are not oppressed. The committee's transportation and sales office will only charge a commission of 2%, without any other fees. A transportation and sales branch will also be established in London. This year's efforts started late and will only focus on preliminary improvements in transportation and sales. In the future, detailed registration methods will also be stipulated for tea firm tea manufacturing, and further benefits will be sought for tea farmers. After the establishment of the committee's transportation and sales office, tea stack talents will be recruited as much as possible to assist. If there are debt relationships, there will also be handling methods. As for tea firms that do not borrow from the committee this year, if their tea is transported and sold by the committee, the tea price obtained after selling all the tea products will be handed over to the original lender after deducting commissions and advances to settle accounts with the tea firm. If the original lender voluntarily recovers the loan, before the products are shipped, the committee may review the qualifications of the tea firm, confirm that it meets the committee's prescribed loan amount, and transfer the loan and interest after verification, so there is no impact on the debts of the tea stacks." (April 3rd)

Suzhou: Zhang Yipeng Requests Commissioner Zang to Pay Attention to Three Matters

Zang Qifang, the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Wuxi District, arrived in Suzhou by car from Shanxi at around 6 PM on the 5th, accompanied by Section Chief Cui Bofu and Xu Jicheng, a strategist from the District Security Command. That evening, Zang visited Zhu Shusheng, the President of the Jiangsu High Court. At 9 AM on the 6th, he convened officials from various agencies and village leaders and patrol officers in Zhongshan Hall for a "Grand Joint Memorial Week" event, attended by five to six hundred people. The event began with a report by Chairman Sun Danchen, followed by a speech from Commissioner Zang, which covered four points: how to cope with the difficulties China is facing, the direction of the central government's efforts, the working goals of local governments, and matters requiring special attention from individuals. Subsequently, Zhang Yipeng, the Director of the Relief Institute, delivered a welcome speech on behalf of the people of Wuxian, and expressed three points for Commissioner Zang to pay attention to: Security issues: At present, bandits are rampant in the four rural areas, and villagers with some wealth are moving to cities. Relief efforts should be strengthened to provide the unemployed in the area with a place to settle, strictly prohibit opening halls to recruit disciples, and eliminate local bullies to cut off the source of bandits. Economic issues: It is necessary to provide relief to farmers, industrialists, and merchants, especially paying attention to farmers. Prohibition of opium: Wuxian has a large population, so there are many opium addicts. The government should be lenient and provide them with ways to quit and start anew, but due to limited funding, opium cessation centers cannot accommodate all addicts, and the fee system has been abolished, leaving those without money unable to quit. There are currently over two thousand opium addicts waiting to quit, and six hundred in cessation centers, so more funds should be raised to benefit opium addicts. The meeting then adjourned. In the afternoon, Commissioner Zang inspected various agencies such as the County Government, Education Bureau, Construction Bureau, and Public Security Bureau. That evening at 7 PM, he was scheduled to convene an administrative meeting at the County Government to discuss everything. He is scheduled to leave Suzhou for the provincial capital this morning.

Rice Industry Requests a Ban on Purchasing Foreign Rice

The Wuxian Grain Industry Guild, upon hearing reports of the authorities planning to purchase foreign rice, specifically submitted a petition to the Provincial Government's Ministry of Internal Affairs on the 5th, stating that China's rice harvest in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and other provinces last year was not poor, and there are sufficient grain reserves. In the autumn of foreign goods dumping, foreign rice should not be allowed to be dumped again. They requested a ban on this.

Kunshan: Scheduled Inspection of All County Inns

The Kunshan Public Security Bureau has organized vocational training courses. Inns, bathhouses, and barber shops throughout the county have completed their training. The bureau has scheduled inspections for inns from April 5th to 10th, bathhouses from April 11th to 14th, and barber shops from April 15th to 25th. The inspection results will be reported to the bureau for rewards and punishments.

Wuxi: Lake Bandits Plan to Disturb Local Areas, Alert

Recently, a large gang of bandits in Zhejiang, allied with lake bandits, totaling over two hundred people, gathered in Taihu Lake, plotting to disturb the area. They plan to land at Wutangmen, Renzigang, and Southern Spring Town in the Wuxi area along the lake to loot. After receiving the warning, County Magistrate Long immediately reported it to the Sixth Brigade of the Provincial Security Force stationed in Wuxi, which promptly dispatched two companies, hiring steamers and civilian boats to be ready at the Gongyun Bridge. After 10 PM, the County Government received a telegram from Southern Spring, stating that the bandit crowd had left the town and was approaching. Gunfire could be faintly heard, requesting prompt dispatch of a team to the countryside for protection. Battalion Commander Zheng, accompanied by Adjutant Wu Junsen and Quartermaster Ma Xianrong, led the team to the countryside. The County Public Security Bureau also dispatched the County Water Patrol Team to the countryside to assist in the suppression. It is also reported that this group of bandits is carrying sixty-nine rifles and four machine guns, having fled into Taihu Lake and Dongting Mountain Lake from Jiaxing and other counties. Yunyan Bridge, the border between Wuxi and Wujin, has also received an alert, and counties along the lake are under strict guard.

Eight County Police Teams Inspected in Wuxi

The Spring Grand Inspection of the Second District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water and Land Public Security Police Team will be held in Wuxi tomorrow (the 8th). Yu Jingtang, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, will personally come to Wuxi to conduct the inspection. The participating troops include the police from Wuxian, Changshu, Wujin, Jiangyin, Wujiang, Taicang, Kunshan, and the Second District Water Police, with a total of 991 soldiers. The Wuxi County Public Security Bureau has arranged Huangnidun City God Temple, Houqijie Great King Temple, Huishan Ancestral Temple, Yanggong Temple, Zhonglie Temple, and Lihuazhuang Yansheng Hall as lodging locations in advance. The chief officers of each inspected troop, such as Zhang from Wuxian, Zhou Ding from Changshu, Xu Shiguang from Wujin, Zhang Ruijing from Jiangyin, and Zhou Weilie from the Water Police District, have arrived in Wuxi. The firearms of the inspected water police officers have also been transported to Wuxi by the Jingping and Zhaowu warships.

Panic Over Excess Copper Coins

Various industries in Wuxi, such as tobacco, alcohol, soy sauce, rickshaws, meat, local products, and candles, are concerned that the market price of copper coins cannot follow the standard set by the Ministry, often hovering around 3,100 coins. The cost of exchange is increasing daily, so they have repeatedly requested the Chamber of Commerce to forward letters to the County Government and the Qianye Guild, requiring them to follow the standard set by the Ministry and use 3,000 coins as the opening price. The County Government has also issued a public notice on record. Subsequently, the Qianye Guild stated that the market price of copper coins fluctuates based on the amount in circulation, which will be limited by requiring the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to uniformly exchange copper coins according to the limited price. The guild resolved that after April [blank] the Qianye Guild will no longer buy or sell copper coins, nor will it discuss exchange rates. Since the market price was limited to 3,000, the amount of copper coins in circulation has greatly increased, but there is nowhere to spend them, causing great panic among various industries. They have successively reported to the Chamber of Commerce, inviting various industries, banks, Qianye Guild, and the County Government to discuss a proper solution to maintain the market.

After Zhenjiang Customs established a branch station in Cheng two years ago, it has now been converted into an upper and lower passenger and cargo station. Changshu: Telephone Charges to Be Collected by Call

The telephone service in the county is a commercial company, founded in 1913 with a capital of 180,000 yuan. However, due to having only 4850 subscribers, it has suffered significant losses for many years. Excluding expenses, the official interest is not enough to cover the debts. Now, in order to make up for the losses, the company plans to collect charges by call, similar to Shanghai. However, it is feared that users will object, so it will seek the consent of the majority of users, or increase the monthly fee. Which option will be implemented will be decided soon.

Haizhou: Overnight Fire on Yuntai Mountain

Yuntai Mountain in Lianyungang City is one of the four famous mountains in Jiangsu, rich in products and excellent in scenery. The local government has long been studying forest management methods for the mountain. Yesterday evening (the 3rd) at about 7 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the forest near Zhangdao Temple on the northern foot of the mountain. The north wind was strong, and the fire spread across the mountainside, illuminating dozens of miles. Nearby residents suspected a bandit alarm, and all the blockhouses fired guns and cannons to warn, with no one daring to go out. The fire was not extinguished until about 10 AM the next morning. According to investigations, the fire area was over a hundred hectares, and the number of burnt trees is countless, estimated to be worth over 100,000 yuan.

Bengbu: Ministry of Finance Maintains Huai Salt Rotation System

Bengbu is a sales port for Huai salt. All salt transported from northern Anhui must be stored in warehouses and sold in rotation, which is the so-called rotation sales system. This system was approved by the Ministry of Finance in 1932 and has been in place for over three years. As it has been implemented for a long time, the accumulated salt is increasing daily, the organization is deficient, and the cost is naturally heavy. The price of salt has risen invisibly, and the burden on consumers has increased. Salt merchants such as Xiang Jinwen believe that northern Anhui is a free sales area, and selling salt in rotation is close to monopoly, which violates the principle of free sales. In recent months, they have repeatedly requested the authorities to abolish the rotation system, but have not been approved. Furthermore, northern Anhui has recently recruited merchants to transport a large amount of stored [blank] and plans to ship [blank] sales, so they submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance, requesting reconsideration. It is reported that the Ministry of Finance has responded clearly, stating in substance that the [blank] transport from Anhui and Henan must still maintain the Bengbu rotation sales method in order to emphasize tax sales. The Bengbu [blank] price has been instructed by the Ministry to the Huaihe [blank] Transport Envoy to order the Bengbu Tax Collection Office to carefully review it, so as to achieve fairness. The Ministry's order to various regions to increase the transport of stored [blank] was originally to adjust supply and demand. Since transport merchants [blank] paid a large amount of taxes, it is inevitable that they must give appropriate treatment to this new tax [blank] in order to [blank] consider. From the above three points, it is difficult to abolish the Bengbu Huai [blank] rotation sales system for the time being.

Xiaoshan: Silkworm Farmers All Feed Improved Species

The Xiaoshan Improved Sericulture Model Area, in order to improve [blank] industry production, yesterday specifically issued a public notice stating that all silkworm farmers must raise improved species. All Yuhang local species, [blank] county local species, silkworm farmers' self-retained local species, and inferior species not distributed in the district have been repeatedly banned by the county. As the sericulture season begins, it is inevitable that merchants seeking profit will come to the district to sell local species. They have ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly investigate and prohibit it, and all silkworm farmers should be aware of this. If there is a sale of local species or other inferior species, once discovered, they will be punished without leniency.

Local News

Song Ziwen Meets with the Press Yesterday

Discussing the Work of the National Economic Council This Year: China's Successful Stabilization of Foreign Exchange Reported; Central Bank Deposits Increased to Over 700 Million

Mr. Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council and Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, received newspaper reporters at the Bank of China at 11:00 AM on the 6th and made the following remarks:

National Economic Council – This Year's Work

According to Mr. Song, the National Economic Council will convene a regular meeting in Beijing at the end of this month or the beginning of next month to report on the general situation of this year's work and to determine the work plan for next year. The Northwest transportation network has been completed this year. The highways from Sichuan to Shaanxi and Gansu have been opened to traffic one after another. This year's health work will focus on Yunnan. Recently, Chairman Chen of Fujian Province also sent a letter requesting the dispatch of personnel to assist in carrying out all tasks. As for water conservancy work, it is handled by the National Water Conservancy Commission, which is presided over by Finance Minister Kong. The main task this year is to block the breaches of the Yellow River.

China Adopts Foreign Exchange Standard

Regarding China's currency system, it has in fact abandoned the silver standard and implemented the foreign exchange standard. The stabilization of foreign exchange has now been successfully achieved. The foreign exchange situation on November 4 remains maintained to this day. The US dollar, shilling, and Japanese gold have not changed much. Therefore, China's foreign exchange does not have a special inclination towards the US dollar, shilling, or Japanese gold. As for whether there will be major changes in the future, we will decide on China's inclination again.

Bank of China Deposits Increase Sharply

The Bank of China was originally government-run, but later became a commercial bank with the addition of a huge amount of commercial shares. Last year, the government increased its official shares, and some people suspected that the Bank of China's deposits would decrease thereafter. But in fact, after the Bank of China increased its official shares, its deposits increased sharply. Last year, deposits totaled more than 766 million yuan, an increase of more than 219 million yuan compared with the previous year, which is the highest record for the Bank of China's deposits. From this, it can be seen that the people's belief in the Bank of China can actually represent the people's belief in the government, which is very different from the past. At the same time, the government's responsibility has also increased. After the government and commerce become one, the government's power is indeed greater, but the responsibility is also heavier. Also, among the Bank of China's deposits last year, there were deposits from various commercial banks, totaling more than 90 million yuan, because all industries were depressed last year and all banks did not dare to make loans.

The Three Banks Issue More Paper Money

The issuance of paper money by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications continues to increase. Previously, the paper money issued by the three banks totaled 700 million yuan, but now it has increased by 120 million yuan. There are three reasons for this: the issuance of paper money by commercial banks has decreased, this is one; people exchange silver for legal tender, this is two; and foreign banks, except for Japanese banks, exchange silver for legal tender, this is three. However, although the issuance of paper money has increased, the reserves are sufficient, so the people's belief is very good. In the future, it will gradually increase as needed. Regarding the storage of silver among the people, there are currently no statistics. Most of the silver in Hebei Province has flowed out, while the storage of silver among the people in Shandong and Henan provinces is still large. As for the Ministry of Finance exchanging 50 million ounces of silver for gold and depositing it in the United States, it is for foreign exchange purposes, because gold can be moved at any time and can be used to purchase any foreign exchange, which is very convenient.

Bank of China Plans to Establish Overseas Branches

Various commercial banks plan to implement a joint system. I have only heard of this and do not know the details. According to my observation of various commercial banks, if they implement a joint system, their strength will increase, which should be better than being separate. However, there are many ways to join forces, such as joint reserves, which is one of them. As for the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, they will still be separate. The Central Bank is being reorganized into a reserve bank, and preparations are still actively underway. I have not heard when it will be established. In addition to its existing branch in London, the Bank of China is currently planning to establish branches in New York, Singapore, San Francisco, Java, and Annam to facilitate remittances. I originally planned to go to various places to inspect the branches, but I was unable to set off due to the currency reform. "Now that I have some free time and the weather is getting warmer, I have decided to set off on a trip to inspect the various places in the short term," he said.

The Government Has Not Borrowed Foreign Debt at Present

There are rumors that the Ministry of Railways plans to borrow 250 million from the banking community. Minister of Railways Zhang Gongquan did not have any contacts in Shanghai. "I have not heard that China plans to borrow from Britain without success, and that Chen Guangfu, general manager of the Shanghai Bank, went to the United States again under orders to contact the United States for loans. Although China had intended to borrow from foreign countries to develop domestic construction, it is not currently underway. Although the US cotton and wheat loan was handled by me before, I have not been involved since I resigned as Minister of Finance, so it is difficult to answer whether it has been repaid or not." At that time, someone asked Mr. Song for his opinion on Japan's proposal of "industrial Japan, agricultural China." Mr. Song smiled and did not answer, instructing that he could inquire with the Sino-Japanese Trade Association. Mr. Song continued, "Some people advocate that banks reduce interest rates to relieve industry and commerce. The national banks, including the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, should first reduce the interest rates on loans to commercial banks. This may be possible, but it depends on the will of the Ministry of Finance."

Yesterday in the Huangpu River, a Japanese Ship Collided with a Chinese Ship

The Tangshan Maru Collided with the Shihe, Causing Significant Damage

The Shihe, a transport ship of the Public Benefit Shipping Company in this port, was violently collided with by the Tangshan Maru, a Japanese ship of the Nisshin Company, in the Huangpu River yesterday. The Shihe's hull was hit, causing huge losses. After our reporter received the news, he went to various parties to investigate. The details of the matter are described as follows:

The Shihe Was About to Sail

The Shihe, a ship of the Public Benefit Shipping Company, weighs 1,513 tons, has a registered net tonnage of 918.27, is 157 feet 8 inches long, 24 feet 3 inches wide, and 15 feet 2 inches deep, has a draft of 17 feet 6 inches, has two decks, a triple expansion engine, 640 horsepower, and travels at 8.5 knots per hour. It was built in Germany in 1903. The ship came to Shanghai with coal this time and was berthed at the river piers 28 and 29 in the Huangpu River. After unloading the coal, it was ready to sail at about 10:00 AM yesterday. The Shihe was about to leave the river pier and head to Haizhou, but it was violently collided with by the Tangshan Maru, a Japanese ship that was entering the port at the time, causing significant damage.

Situation at the Time of the Collision

The Tangshan Maru of the Nisshin Company, which now sails from Nanhua to Shanghai and also sails the Northern Seas line, has a capacity of 2,089 tons. It had just loaded a large number of goods and passengers from Guangdong and other ports and returned to Shanghai. At about 10:00 AM yesterday, when it was approaching the Huangpu River surface of the power plant, it passed the river piers 28 and 29, just as the Shihe was turning around to leave the buoy and was about to sail. Suddenly, a sailboat came from the river. The Tangshan Maru was afraid of colliding with the sailboat, so it gave way slightly. However, the pressure of the tide was very great. The bow of the Tangshan Maru avoided the sailboat, but took advantage of the momentum to collide with the stern of the Shihe, causing a loud bang and a major disaster.

Extremely Serious Damage

At the time when the Shihe was hit, it had not yet left the river pier. The captain saw the bow of the Tangshan Maru sailing sideways, and because his ship was moored on the side of the river pier, there was no way to avoid it. He had to immediately raise a black flag, indicating that he was asking the other ship to stop immediately, otherwise a huge danger would occur. However, it was too late. The bow of the Tangshan Maru had violently collided with the left side of the stern of the Shihe. The stern of the Shihe was immediately broken, and the steel plates were torn in many places. The hole was one zhang square, and the buildings and railings on the stern deck were all destroyed, causing extremely heavy losses.

Joint Survey by Both Parties

After the accident, the Tangshan Maru immediately sailed back to the wharf to unload goods and passengers. The captain of the Shihe immediately reported to the Yihe Company, the agent of the ship in Shanghai. The company first sent personnel to the ship to inspect the damage, and then ordered the captain to submit a report and submit it to the Maritime Affairs Bureau and the insurance company, asking them to send surveyors to the ship to survey. At that time, he also ordered the Shihe to suspend its departure and stay in Shanghai for major repairs. In the afternoon, the ship surveyors of the insurance company had gone to the Shihe and Tangshan Maru to inspect the ships. It is said that the damage to the Tangshan Maru was very minor. The issue of responsibility for the collision is currently difficult to discuss.

Liu Luyin and Cheng Tiangu Still Stay in Shanghai; Wei Daoming Visited Wang Again Yesterday to Report

Silk Manufacturers Plan to Establish Artificial Silk Factory

Capital of 10 Million Yuan, Half Government and Half Commercial; The Factory Plans to be Located in Hangzhou, Zhejiang

According to Shenshi News Agency, China's silk industry was once very developed. In recent years, it has been hit by the world's economic downturn and competition from artificial silk, and its situation has plummeted. It is found that artificial silk is an important raw material for silk production and is purely imported from abroad. There are no factories in China specializing in its manufacture. In view of this, silk manufacturers in this city have drawn up a plan and submitted it to the central government to establish an artificial silk factory. Preparations are now actively underway. The details are as follows:

Preparation Process

Because silk merchants in this city believe that the annual leakage of artificial silk is very large, they have drawn up a plan and asked Representative Wang Yansong to take it to Beijing and submit it to the Administrative and Industrial Departments to raise funds to establish a national artificial silk factory. It is heard that Minister of Finance Kong is very much in favor of this plan and has agreed to assist. Mr. Wang made satisfactory contacts in Beijing and immediately began preparations to raise funds after returning to Shanghai. It is heard that a certain amount of funds has already been raised.

Outline of the Plan

The planned capital of the factory is tentatively set at 10 million national currency, half government and half commercial. The government shares will be allocated by the government in one lump sum, while the commercial shares can be raised in the silk industry. The location of the factory is generally in Hangzhou, which is convenient for transportation. As for technical talents, there is still a shortage at the time of opening, and only foreign talents can be borrowed. Later, outstanding students from the Department of Chemistry and the Department of Textile Engineering of domestic universities will be selected to study in Europe and the United States, and they can be hired when they return. In addition, encouraging exports and expanding sales channels are all included in the plan. It is expected that when this plan is realized in the future, it will definitely be able to recover a part of the rights and interests.

Japanese Merchants Set Up Cotton Mills in North China – Chinese Cotton Yarn is in Greater Danger

Japanese-Funded Cotton Mill in Tianjin Scheduled to Start Construction on the 15th; 90% of Transactions at the Cotton Yarn Exchange are Japanese Yarn

The Japanese cotton yarn industry has gained a special position of development in China. Recently, it has been protected by the government's policy of maintaining industry. A large-scale cotton mill has been established in Tianjin, and contacts have been established with factories in Shanghai, Qingdao, Wuhan, and other places. The Chinese cotton yarn market, which is already on its last breath, will be in greater danger. Because this matter concerns China's entire cotton yarn industry, the reporter has inquired with various parties concerned about the process. The details are as follows:

Japanese Cotton Yarn Factory in North China Will Start Construction

There are six Chinese-funded cotton mills in Tianjin, including Yuyuan, Hengyuan, Beiyang, Baocheng, Yudai, and Huaxin. In recent years, due to the decline of the cotton yarn industry and the difficulty of economic turnover, the Japanese merchants have bought out two of them, Yudai and Yuyuan. It is found that the Japanese merchants have cotton mills in Shanghai, Qingdao, and Hankou, but there are no cotton mills in Tianjin. Recently, in order to further expand the cotton yarn industry in China and manipulate the domestic market, the Toyo Cotton Mill, Osaka Spinning Co., and Zhongbo Spinning Co. have jointly established a new factory in Dongju, Tianjin. It is scheduled to start construction on the 15th. The first step of the plan is to equip 50,000 spindles, and the second step is to complete the increase of spindles to 100,000 by next year. In the future, when this plan is realized, not only will the original Chinese-funded cotton mills in Tianjin be controlled by it, but China's entire cotton yarn industry will also become a nest of overturned eggs, and there will be no one who can compete with the four enemies.

Comparison of the Number of Chinese and Japanese Spindles

Comparing the spindles of Chinese and Japanese cotton mills, there are currently about 2.7 million spindles in Chinese-funded cotton mills across the country. Because Chinese factories have difficulty in terms of raw material costs, interest rates, and capital liquidity, they have now reduced 3.5% (that is, 35% have been stopped). Although the current situation has seen a turnaround, it is still strong on the outside and weak on the inside. Japanese-funded cotton mills in Shanghai, Qingdao, and Hankou have about 2.45 million spindles. Because of the improvement of their products, the low cost of interest, and the smooth sales,

Page 10

flourishing, the Japanese-funded cotton mills in Shanghai are working day and night to catch up with production, and they are still worried that the orders will not be enough to allocate. In contrast, it is truly chilling.

90% of Market Transactions are Japanese Yarn

The Shanghai Chinese Cotton Yarn Exchange on Edward Road has officially announced the opening of Japanese yarn since August 1 last year. In just over nine months, Japanese yarns such as Chenfeng from the Rihua Factory, Toyonen from the Toyota Factory, Shuiyue and Caiqiu from the Neiwaimian Factory, Sunlight from the Shanghai Factory, Binlai and Wuma from the Qingdao Gongda Factory, and others have accounted for more than 70% to 80% of the transactions in the market. The only Chinese yarns that can barely maintain their position in the market are Zhongren from the Shenxin Factory and a few others. In order to learn from the past and avoid future mistakes, if a few more days pass, I am afraid that Chinese yarn will not be able to maintain its position. Although it is now the time of Sino-Japanese relations adjustment and economic cooperation, the government and merchants are urged to rescue and protect this last remaining industry.

North and South Power Plants Implement Power Supply Plan

Chinese Merchants Plan to Expand 130,000 Kilowatts; Zhabei Transmits Electricity to Jiading and Taicang along the Sihukou Road The rural power supply plan of the Shanghai Chinese Electrical Company has been gradually implemented. In the future, after the new factory is completed, it will be expanded from 30,000 kilowatts to 130,000 kilowatts, which can supply power to a circle of 100 kilometers. The Zhabei Hydropower Plant will also transmit electricity to Jiading along the Sihukou Road. The details are as follows, which were obtained by the reporter of Dagong News Agency:

Purchase New Machines to Increase Power

The machines and boilers required for the company's new power plant were ordered from the German Siemens factory in October last year, including two 15,000-kilowatt steam turbine generators, and two boilers were ordered from the British Babgok Factory. One boiler was ordered from the Czech Skoda Factory. Each boiler has a steam capacity of 70 tons and a steam pressure of 40 atmospheres. Other equipment such as distribution boards, transformer manufacturing water equipment, boiler electrical management, and coal addition equipment have also been contracted one after another. The total value of the above is 163,777 pounds sterling, equivalent to more than 2.7 million legal currency. The factory building design has reserved space for the installation of the third steam turbine generator and the fourth boiler in the future. Therefore, the future power generation capacity of the new factory can be increased from 30,000 kilowatts to 45,000 kilowatts without the need for additional piling and factory construction. The area of the factory base can accommodate the expansion of capacity to 130,000 kilowatts in the future. As for high-voltage voltages, there are two types: one is 5,500 volts, which is specially used for the existing high-voltage power transmission in the Hukun District, and the other is 33,000 volts, which is prepared for long-distance rural town high-voltage power transmission. In the future, when the new factory is completed and managed properly, the coal used for each degree of power generation will be reduced by at least 40% compared with the current coal used for power generation.

Extend the Route to Supply Power to the Countryside

In addition to the 30,000-volt high-voltage overhead wire, the 5,500-volt high-voltage overhead wire has been extended by 21 kilometers and 239 meters. Those that have been connected to provide power include Beiqiao, Puji Nursing Home, Zhuanqiao, Xingci Electric Factory, Zhujiagang Town, Changqiao Town, Gangko Town, Meilong Town, Hongqiao Town, Dongcaohejing, Hongqiao Road, 996 Alley, Hongqiao New Village, Caohe Temple, Xinlonghua, Zhengjiaqiao, Xinqiaocun, Xinqiao New Village, Tongjiazai, Minhang, and other places. Those that are still in progress but have not yet been electrified include Songjiang Electric Company and Zhupu Electric Lamp Factory. Those that are still being planned include Caohang Town, Huajing Town, Mingang Town, and Rose Garden New Village. When the power generation capacity is increased to 130,000 kilowatts in the future, it can supply electricity to a radius of 100 kilometers.

Zhabei Power Plant's Power Transmission Plan

In addition, the Huashang Zhabei Hydropower Company has provided electricity to Doushan, Dachang, Luodian, and other places to support rural construction in the past. Last year, the company responded to the needs of electric lamp factories in Jiading and Taicang counties and decided to carry out the same power transmission plan. The contract is still being signed. The first step of the project is to lay pole wires along the Sihukou Highway. After both parties agree on the power supply fee, it will be opened and implemented on a regular basis.

The Chang'an Steamer of the Sanbei Company, en route upstream to Hankou, passed Jiujiang on the morning of the 4th. Some passengers had not paid for their tickets or food. According to regulations, meals were no longer provided to them. Unexpectedly, when lunch was served, these passengers, disregarding the rules, demanded food from the kitchen. Upon arriving at Wuxue, the ship owner reported the incident to the local Public Security Bureau, who sent police onboard to arrest the two perpetrators. Eurasia Aviation Corporation: Shanghai-Lanzhou Route Schedule Change

Eastbound flights now every Thursday, same time.

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Lanzhou mail plane, originally scheduled to fly westbound on Tuesdays and Fridays and eastbound on Wednesdays and Saturdays, has changed its eastbound schedule to every Thursday due to connections with the Shaanxi-Yunnan route. Flight times remain the same. This allows passengers from Yunnan and Sichuan to transfer to the mail plane at the Xi'an station and arrive in Shanghai on the same day. The company's regulations for carrying passengers and cargo to Tianshui, Liangzhou, Pingliang, Hengzhou, Luoyang, Taiyuan, and other locations, after obtaining special approval, will continue to be implemented as before.

Representatives from the Ministry of Industries' Shanghai offices, as well as Yu Zuoting, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, represented by Zheng Chengqing, and Dr. Pan Jianliang, representative of the Rice and Wheat Improvement Institute, were at the dock to welcome them. Ministry of Finance Approves Tax Exemption for Export of Antique Porcelain Replicas

Reply to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, to promote the export of national porcelain, sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance on February 6, requesting exemption from porcelain export taxes. The Federation received reply telegram No. 3939 from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, approving that antique porcelain replicas be treated as ordinary porcelain and exempted from tax. The original telegram stated: "To the Shanghai National Federation of Chambers of Commerce: The telegram of [date] regarding the request from overseas porcelain merchants such as Meicheng Porcelain Company to completely exempt porcelain export taxes has been noted. Previously, these merchants submitted a report to the Ministry, which was instructed to be reviewed by the Customs Administration through the Chief Inspectorate of Customs. The Ministry has further investigated that porcelain exports are currently tax-exempt under existing export regulations. The reason for taxing as antiques or antique porcelain replicas is due to the ancient dynastic marks and images on the porcelain. To alleviate the difficulties of merchants and maintain foreign trade in the porcelain industry, it is specifically stipulated that porcelain reported for export, if manufactured individually or in pairs and intended to be sold at high prices as antiques, should be taxed as antiques or antique porcelain replicas. However, porcelain manufactured in large quantities, even if bearing ancient dynastic marks and images to increase sales prices, will be considered porcelain and exempted from tax under item 233 of the export tariff. This order is issued by the Ministry for compliance and notification, and you are hereby notified. Stamped by the Ministry of Finance."

Two Railway Bureaus Preparing for Opening Ceremony of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway

Entire Project to be Completed by End of the Month, Official Opening on May 1st

The Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, built by the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, has completed its bridge construction after more than a month of work. Track laying is more than halfway complete and is expected to be fully completed by the end of this month. The official opening is scheduled for May 1st. The two railway bureaus are preparing for an opening ceremony and have invited Minister of Railways Zhang Jia'ao to preside over the event. The Jiaxing station of the line will be located at the existing Jiaxing station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. However, due to insufficient platform space, it will be extended by thirty yards. In addition, due to the increased station services, the Jiaxing station will be upgraded to a first-class station.

The Bureau has formulated measures to ban colored tea, which have been distributed to tea merchants in various regions. The Shanghai Tea Trade Association has been commissioned to invent and manufacture non-toxic colorings. The factory is scheduled to begin production of non-toxic colorings tomorrow, which will be promoted for adoption by tea merchants throughout the region. Anyone who does not use improved colorings will be banned from exporting upon inspection.

The robbers resisted arrest and opened fire, injuring more than thirteen passers-by. Although the detective force fired openly, it was in a busy street with many pedestrians, which was extremely dangerous. In the future, the Municipal Council should instruct the patrol officers to take into account the lives of pedestrians and exercise caution when firing shots. The Shanghai First Special District Local Court is requested to forward this letter to the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council, stating that in the future, when shooting thieves on the streets, serious consideration should be given to the lives of pedestrians to avoid innocent deaths and injuries to as many as thirteen people. Jiangsu Provincial Government Seeks to Revitalize the Rural Areas, Improve Cooperative Enterprises

Each county will hold two training sessions per year, hiring experts to give lectures and cultivate members' knowledge.

Shanghai County Magistrate Ye Zhendong has returned to the county after visiting Chairman Chen in the province and requesting instructions on boosting the rural economy and improving the overall cooperative enterprise. It is reported that the Jiangsu Provincial Government, recognizing that cooperative enterprises in the province are not yet widespread, resulting in cooperative knowledge not being deeply rooted among the people, and that existing cooperatives are suffering from business decline due to a lack of capable personnel to manage them, has formulated measures to vigorously improve cooperative enterprises in each county. It has ordered each county to hold two cooperative training sessions each year, with each session lasting two weeks, hiring experts to give lectures. All cooperative staff must attend the lectures. At the end of the session, an examination will be held, and those who pass will be issued certificates to expand cooperative enterprises, thereby boosting the rural economy and stabilizing rural society.

Hou Shipei, No. 351, and Li Rongsheng, No. 37, ticket sellers of the British-owned Public Bus Company, both having served for two years, recently conceived evil intentions. Zhang Maogou Wounded by Chopping, the Inside Story Has Been Ascertained, Clan Dispute Over Land, Instigating Criminals to Harm

Zhang Maogou, a local resident living in a flat on Chaoyang Road, worked at the Huitong Cotton Mill. On the evening of the 3rd of this month, at around 9 PM, he was attacked with knives and axes by enemies in a nearby wasteland, sustaining injuries to his head, legs, and buttocks. The assailants fled in all directions. Zhang collapsed in a pool of blood, barely alive. His mother, Xu, reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station, which dispatched detectives to the scene. The detectives learned that the assailants were Ding Cailang from Tongzhou, who was hiding at 29 Delhi Road, Wupulu, and others. They secretly went to the scene and arrested them. The mastermind, Zhang Quanfa, a local resident, was also apprehended. He was from the same clan as the victim and the dispute arose from a struggle over ancestral land. He had instigated an unknown accomplice to carry out the vicious attack and harm the victim's life. The detectives also went to 56 Chaoyang Road and arrested Zhang Quanfa. It was learned that he was a foreman at the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council. He was also taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Zhang Shizhu, the Municipal Council's lawyer, presented the case, requesting an extension for detailed investigation. Zhang Xu, the mother of the victim, stated that the defendant, Zhang Quanfa, was indeed from the same clan and that the dispute was over a piece of land. During the recent Tomb Sweeping Festival, he forbade Zhang Maogou from going to burn ghost money, claiming that he controlled the land and refused to let the victim do so. He also instigated the defendant Ding Cailang to lure her son to that place to harm him. Judge Xiao ordered the two defendants to be questioned separately. Ding Cailang confessed that he had approached Zhang Quanfa seeking business, who told him that he had a feud with his clan brother, Zhang Maogou. He gave him two yuan and took out a sharp knife and an axe, ordering Ding and an unknown accomplice to go to the open space near the victim's house. Ding lured the victim out, and the unknown accomplice used the axe to hack at him, causing him to fall to the ground. Ding only stabbed the victim's legs four times with a small knife. He did not know the reason for their actions. Zhang Quanfa denied instigating Ding Cailang to harm Zhang Maogou, his other statements were evasive. Judge Xiao ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody for 14 days pending further investigation after the victim recovers from his injuries.

Yesterday's Weather Was Extremely Hot, Highest Temperature 82.9 Degrees

Yesterday's weather in the city was extremely hot, with a maximum temperature of 82.9 degrees and a minimum of 55.4 degrees. The maximum temperature for the same period last year was 62.2 degrees and the minimum was 49.3 degrees. Compared to the past few days, it was as if two different seasons had passed. Pedestrians on the road found their cotton clothes completely unsuitable. In the afternoon, they changed to lined shirts or even single-layer clothing. Due to the sultry heat, many workers were covered in sweat. Servers in taverns and teahouses bared their chests and stomachs, as if overwhelmed by the extreme heat. This phenomenon is unprecedented in recent years and is caused by the passage of a low-pressure system.

Zhang Xinghai, from Peiping, lives at 8, Lane 108 (Longzhi Li), at the intersection of Kang Nao Tuo Road and Dongjing Road in Shanghai West. He is currently a Chinese Detective Chief at the Hongkou Police Station of the Public Concession. Yesterday morning, at around 8:50 AM, just minutes after Zhang left home for work at the police station after having breakfast, four thugs broke into his home and robbed it at will. Zhang's family members were still upstairs at the time. Three of the four thugs were armed with pistols. They rushed up the stairs as soon as they entered the house, directly into Zhang's bedroom. They first threatened Zhang's female relatives with guns, then bound them one by one and confined them to a room, assigning one thug to guard them. The remaining thugs began to search everywhere, ransacking boxes and chests, turning the house upside down, and looting everything in sight for about half an hour before escaping by the same route. Shortly after, Zhang's family members managed to free themselves and urgently called Zhang's office, requesting him to return home immediately. After an inventory, it was discovered that they had been robbed of two pairs of gold bracelets, two pairs of gold earrings, eight gold rings, 500 yuan in silver dollars, and over 600 yuan in paper currency, totaling over 3,120 yuan. They filed a detailed loss report with the Gordon Road Police Station, which has jurisdiction. Chief Chinese Detective Zhu Mengwei led detectives to the scene for investigation. Numerous fingerprints were discovered at the scene, and each one was photographed and taken back to the police station for filing. Dedicated detectives were assigned to search for the thugs and bring them to justice.

Afterwards, I got dozens of yuan in reward, and so on. Content of the Mediation Plan

Yong'an Real Estate Company will be compensated with 1,000 yuan of Jiangzhe Bank stocks held as collateral. Respectfully submitted by the bankrupt Xu Qizhong.

Teng Gu's German "A Brief History of Chinese Painting" Published

In order to promote the characteristics of Chinese painting in Europe, the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition specially invited Dr. Teng Gu to write a book in German, "A Brief History of Chinese Painting," which is more than 200 pages long. Its contents include Chapter 1: Ancient Painting, Chapter 2: The Era of Buddhist Importation, Chapter 3: The Formation of Literati Painting and Court Painting, Chapter 4: The Rebirth of Literati Painting, Eclectic Tendencies and Their Reaction, Chapter 5: Eclecticism and Modern Extremism, and Conclusion. The original manuscript of the book was reviewed by Mr. Cai Yuanpei, who expressed his satisfaction. It was brought to Berlin by Representative Liu Haisu the year before last. At that time, due to the large number of illustrations, printing took time. Therefore, the Preparatory Committee of the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition donated the original manuscript to the Chinese Academy of the Frank Institute in Germany. Now the Chinese Academy has published Teng's work, and the printing is very exquisite.

Shen Jinquan Forcibly Abducted His Cousin for Friends to Violate She Was Detained for Twelve Days Before Escaping She Was Detained and Sent to Court and the Verdict is Pending

Shen Wensheng, a villager of Shenjiawan Shenjiazai in Zhabei, has a daughter named Lianying, who is 19 years old this year. She is quite beautiful. Shen loves her like a jewel in his palm, and is determined to choose a good husband before marrying her. Therefore, she has not been selected for a long time. Shen's cousin, Shen Jinquan, is a driver for the Southern Automobile Company. He is used to wandering and does not know etiquette. He has a close friendship with a colleague named A Quan. He often invites him to play at home. A Quan sees Lianying's beautiful face and covets her beauty. He often thinks of himself as a son-in-law and once asked Shen Jinquan and Jinquan's brother Jinrong to plot to marry her. However, he was despised by Shen Wensheng and his good dream was difficult to achieve. Therefore, he sought second best and wanted to have an affair to fulfill his long-cherished wish. He sought advice from Shen Jinquan. It is shocking that Jinquan disregarded everything and designed to hire a car in advance as an act of forced abduction. Because Lianying works in the Gongda Yarn Factory, she must go out. It is a good plan to start on the way. As a result, at 9 a.m. on February 17, Lianying and her cousin Jinlian were walking together, half a mile away from home, when Shen Jinquan came out to stop her, half-luring and half-forcing her into the car and driving away. Jinlian watched her sister go, and kept silent. But Lianying was taken to a secret room. A Quan arrived and quenched his thirst and thoughts. This happened for twelve days. Her body was violently broken and her lower body was severely injured. She was rushed to the hospital for treatment in a hurry. After she was slightly recovered, she was led back to hide. Guessing her intention, she wanted to use the fait accompli method to make Shen Wensheng agree. Unexpectedly, on April 1, A Quan went out on business and the defense was relatively loose. Shen Lianying, unable to bear the pain, thought that the opportunity had come. She escaped and ran to her aunt's house, crying and telling the previous situation. After being sent home, Shen Wensheng twisted Shen Jinrong to the police station and handed him over to Shen Jinquan, and sent them together to the local court. Shen Jinrong was released on bail, and Shen Jinquan was detained. On the one hand, Shen Wensheng filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Court for abduction and rape. Yesterday, Judge Wu Xiangzu heard the case. Shen Lianying confessed the same situation as before, and Shen Jinlian proved the situation at that time. When questioned, the defendant said that Shen Wensheng borrowed money and failed, and set up this trap out of resentment. Under the official order to start the debate, and based on Shen Lianying's confession that her lower body was injured, she ordered a forensic examination and said, "The debate is over, and the verdict will be heard later. The defendant will be remanded in custody," and it was decided that the hearing will be resumed on the 20th of this month.

Poor People Stole Manure and Became Violent, Beating and Injuring the Inspector Workers of the Cleaning Station

Recently, the cleaning station in Yinxiang District, Zhabei, has found that the manure stored in the toilets in Zhangjia Lane, Derun Road, and other places has been stolen by poor people from other provinces. Therefore, it sent manure workers to strengthen the inspection and prevention. Yesterday afternoon, the manure workers found someone stealing stored manure in the toilet on Derun Road and reported it to the station inspector, who went to intervene. They were beaten by a crowd of poor people from other provinces. The manure workers and inspectors were outnumbered and injured. Afterwards, the police station found a perpetrator and sent him to the station for interrogation. The details are as follows:

Stealing Manure

The cleaning station in Yinxiang District, Zhabei, is contracted by merchants and pays fees on a monthly basis. The station has set up more than ten toilets in Zhangjia Lane, Derun Road, and other places in the district to facilitate residents' storage of manure, killing two birds with one stone. The station's manure is usually transported to Wuxi, Changzhou, and other places, where farmers purchase it for fertilizing the fields. Recently, the station discovered that the manure stored in the toilets was stolen by poor people from other provinces. It was found that Xiao Qilong, Xiao Kouzi, Daba Zi, and Er Mazi were instigating it. It was not investigated. Therefore, it sent manure worker Zhao Deyuan (from Gaoyou, 43 years old, living at No. 2, Xiangshan Lane, Wuhua Road) to strengthen the inspection and prevention.

Poor People Became Violent

At about 2 p.m. yesterday afternoon, Zhao found someone stealing manure in the toilet on Derun Road, packing it in buckets and transporting it privately. According to reports, inspector Dong Xingen (from Shanghai, 38 years old) went to the scene with Zhao. The thieves abandoned the manure buckets and fled in all directions. Zhao took several manure buckets back to the station for temporary placement. This aroused the anger of the poor people from other provinces, who gathered more than 20 people and rushed to beat Dong and Zhao with shoulder poles. Dong and Zhao were outnumbered and injured in the waist, head, shoulders, and back. Their clothes and hats were covered with manure. Fortunately, the Linping Road Police Station in charge of the area received the report and sent police to the scene, arresting the main culprit, Chen Linfa (also known as Er Mazi, from Funing, 45 years old, living in a thatched shed No. 88, Pingmin Village), and brought him to the station for interrogation. The remaining criminals fled and were not caught.

The Criminal Was Sent to the Station

According to the interrogation at the police station, inspector Dong Xingen and manure worker Zhao Deyuan of the cleaning station stated that Chen and the other fugitives, Xiao Qilong, Daba Zi, Xiao Kouzi, etc., instigated poor people from other provinces to steal manure. It was not uncommon. In order to settle the matter, they did not investigate. This time, because they went to intervene, they were violently beaten by Chen and others. They demanded severe punishment. When Chen Linfa was interrogated, he cunningly denied stealing manure and fighting. The police station, because the case involved accusations of theft and injury, and involved criminal prosecution, sent a document to the station along with the three plaintiffs and defendants for interrogation.
