Chen Ruifu's Concubine Acquisition Leads to a Series of Family Troubles

Wife Initially Accuses Him of Adultery Without Success, Now Petitions the Court for Divorce

Chen Ruifu, a native of Ningbo and a senior staff member at the Renji Road Yingli Import and Export Company, residing at No. 50, Zhen De Fang, Baoding Road, Huishan Road, married Wang Minghua (currently 31 years old), a woman from Ningbo, in 1926 through a matchmaker. For a decade, their relationship was considered harmonious, but they had no children. Recently, Wang Minghua suddenly noticed that her husband's behavior had changed drastically, becoming abnormal, ambitious, and not returning home at night. She began to investigate and discovered that her husband

Had an Affair

and was cohabitating with Wu Lingzi, a 23-year-old woman from Hangzhou, at No. 47, Shufeng South Lane, Baoding Road. Consequently, on February 21st of this year, she reported this information to the Huishan Police Station, who dispatched officers to apprehend Chen Ruifu and Wu Lingzi together and bring them to the First Special Court. Under interrogation, Chen Ruifu admitted to taking Wu Lingzi as a concubine, and it was also learned that Wang Minghua had long been aware of this. As a result, the court

Declared Chen Ruifu and Wu Lingzi Innocent in the case. Now, Wang Minghua has hired lawyer E Sen and filed a petition with the civil division of the First Special Court, requesting a divorce from her husband Chen Ruifu and an order for him to pay alimony. Yesterday afternoon, around 2 p.m., judge Tao Dejun presided over the hearing in the Seventh Civil Court. The plaintiff, Chen Wang Minghua, accompanied by lawyer E Sen, appeared in court and stated that the defendant, Chen Ruifu, had committed adultery with another woman, Wu Lingzi, and that the plaintiff had reported this to the Huishan Police Station, who arrested them and brought them to the criminal court of this court for trial. The defendant also confessed in court, so the

Facts of the Case have already been recorded in the criminal court's records. She requested the court to investigate and retrieve the case file for clarification. She also stated that although the defendant's family is wealthy, before the division of property, his economic power rested with her. Therefore, when he was engaged in business outside, he often needed funds, which the plaintiff provided assistance with. However, since last year, after receiving a portion of his inheritance from his father, he has treated the plaintiff as worthless, not only failing to return the borrowed jewelry but also ceasing to provide living expenses. Instead, he

Embraced New Love and did not remember the past hardships, clearly severing their marital bond. This aligns with the provisions of Article 1052, Section 2 of the Civil Code, which pertains to adultery. Therefore, she requested the court to order a divorce between the two parties, to order the defendant to return the borrowed jewelry worth 15,000 yuan, to order the return of the plaintiff's inherent property worth 4,500 yuan, to order the defendant to pay the plaintiff alimony at a rate of 150 yuan per month until she reaches the age of sixty, totaling

54,000 Yuan, and to order the defendant to bear the costs of this lawsuit, etc. The defendant, Chen Ruifu, did not appear but sent lawyer Yuan Yang'an as his representative to defend the case. He argued that the plaintiff and defendant had been married for ten years and their relationship had been harmonious. The only reason he took a concubine was because the plaintiff could not bear children, for the sake of continuing the family line, and to live together permanently with shared wealth. The plaintiff was already aware of this and did not object. Therefore, the criminal court declared him innocent.

According to Civil Law Article 1053, "A party with the right to claim based on the circumstances in sections 1 and 2 of the preceding article may not request a divorce if they have agreed to it in advance, condoned it afterward, or if more than six months have passed since becoming aware of it, or if more than two years have passed since the occurrence of the circumstances." He also stated that he was unable to afford alimony. Therefore, he requested that the court

Dismiss the Plaintiff's lawsuit. Moreover, since both parties are intellectuals, he requested that the court persuade the plaintiff to reconcile, etc. The plaintiff's lawyer, E, further stated that regarding the issue of infertility, it had been verified by a doctor that the defendant was actually infertile, and the fault was not with the plaintiff, etc. Judge Tao reviewed the evidence and decided to persuade the plaintiff. The case was rescheduled for further hearing on the afternoon of the 23rd, and both lawyers were instructed to attempt a reconciliation.

At the time of the accident, Wang was sound asleep with her three-year-old son, Xiaomao. Pig Boat Robbed in Broad Daylight

Live Pigs and Bedding Stolen

On the 2nd of this month, the Jiangbei pig boat Ye Xizhang loaded one hundred and ninety-nine live pigs from Zhang Dalin and other customers from the Nihetai pig market in Zhanghuanggang and came to Songjiang for sale. After two hours, they stole thirty-five fresh pigs and bedding, etc., and sailed north and escaped. Professor Zhou Huan's book on political parties in Europe and the United States is published

The content is divided into six parts: Britain, the United States, France, Germany, Russia, and Italy, totaling 100,000 words. It explains the party platform, policies, rise and fall, and the rise and fall of the various political parties in these six advanced countries, as well as the conspiracies, riots, and diplomatic events without omission. The materials are rich and the arguments are clear and understandable. Not only can it be used for research by political scientists, but it can also be used as a reference for those engaged in political movements in China. Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Xiao Bai)

Everything in the world is constantly changing.

"Water that does not flow becomes stagnant." Similarly, the development and progress of all undertakings will inevitably lag behind and fail if we do not constantly pay attention to improving and innovating, and strive to make them new every day.

"Progress" is the characteristic that everyone should have in this turbulent era, because "if you don't advance, you retreat." We should always be afraid of falling behind and being abandoned and destroyed in the fierce competition for survival.

However, many people often think that the improvement of everything in society is holistic and sudden, and they do not understand the principle of focusing on the big picture and starting with the small details. In fact, we can only achieve final success by starting with the small details and gradually finding ways to improve and evolve.

"Gradual change" leads to "sudden change." This is what philosophy tells us.

Nomadic Life in the City

— Zhu Ying

In our metropolis, the "Paris of the East," people of the upper, middle, and lower classes all live somewhat like nomads who move according to water and grass.

First, let's talk about the upper class. Although the upper class lives in large Western-style houses with gardens in front and lawns in back, heaven knows if they spend one or two nights in these houses out of ten days. Usually, they spend the night in one hotel today, then stay in another hotel tomorrow, and naturally switch to yet another hotel the day after tomorrow. Even if they don't stay in hotels, there are many other places to stay. The small mansions of the second and third concubines are also available. If these places become tiresome, they might as well go to a brothel and stay for one or two nights. If it's a Saturday night, they can dance or gamble all night, without worrying about where to spend the night.

The middle class, although not as absolutely unsettled as the upper class, must at least change their residence according to the seasons. For example, in winter, they live in the house, but in summer, they have to lie in rattan chairs on the balcony or in the alleyway to avoid the heat and bedbugs in the house. Some simply take a straw mat and seek a good dream on the sidewalk next to the street. They only return to the house after the weather cools down. And people in this class may sometimes spend one or two nights in a hotel at the beginning of the month when they get paid, gambling and playing with women, and temporarily abandoning their fixed family life.

As for the lower class, they are absolutely unsettled. In summer, they lie under vegetable sheds; in winter, they lie at the entrance of alleys. In addition, bathhouses, porridge shops, boiler rooms, swallow's nests, etc., are all good places to avoid the cold and spend the night. If they have some money to spare, they can spend a dozen cents to occupy a bunk in a small inn. Most of these people play the flute in "Shanghai," begging for food everywhere. Today they are in Yangshupu, tomorrow in Caojiadu, and the day after tomorrow they mix into Gaochang Temple. Their whereabouts are uncertain, and they are content with whatever comes their way, living a completely nomadic life.

Originally, anyone who wants to make a living in Shanghai is actually not much different from the nomadic people who move according to water and grass.

The Ruins of Wu Zicheng

— Fan Fei

After finishing my classes, I went to Wu Yuan for tea and ran into my old classmate Jiang Dayi, whom I hadn't seen in more than three years. After a few brief greetings, he opened a paper bag and pointed to the animal bones, ox horns, pottery shards, and carbonized wood pieces inside, saying, "These things are about the same age as the Most Holy Teacher." Then he said, "These things were found at Wang Feiji." I asked him about the cause and effect of obtaining these things, and he gave the following account: Based on the history of Wang Feiji, Jiang concluded that the palace of Zhang Shicheng at the end of the Yuan Dynasty, the palace of the King of Wu during the Warring States period, and Wu Zicheng were all in this area, so he began to investigate. One day, behind the park, the Jincheng Bank was under major construction. Ming and Qing porcelain shards were found in the excavated soil. Next to a newly dug pit about five cubic meters deep, the silt dug from the pit was piled up. In this silt, animal bones, ox horns (related to ancient people's food), geometric pattern ancient pottery shards, and black pigment pottery shards were found. After obtaining these culturally significant items and studying them, it became clear that they were relics from the Warring States period, and the site of Wu Zicheng was also confirmed. However, due to regulations on the excavation of antiquities, it is not possible to excavate immediately and understand the underground situation. When the relevant academic institutions and people from all countries have a plan and excavate layer by layer, there will be some amazing results.

Can it Withstand this Storm?

Swapping the Nest, Luan and Phoenix

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Prologue: Appreciating Chrysanthemums Near Double Ninth Festival, Seeking Tranquility in a Small Gathering; Recalling Old Dreams with Linked Pearls, Drinking Bitter Tears for Thousands of Autumns

Dabai separated a long leaf and searched for a long time before picking a small stem of flowers and handing it to me. I looked at the flower. The long flower stem was somewhat like a small Western begonia. The petals were purple, and the flower bud was like a small sachet, very exquisite. I brought it to my nose and smelled it. It had a fragrance that was stronger than orchids. I concentrated for a while, clapped my hands, and said, "Now I understand. This is a famous Western flower called violet, and there is a sad and beautiful myth about it." Dabai said, "Isn't everything here inside and out violets? So this small garden has become the Violet Hermitage. When these flowers are in full bloom in April and May, the fragrance fills the alley, and Brother Lan is most proud of it." I said, "Brother Lan loves violets most in his life. No matter what he does, he always brings this up. You can say that he has an affinity for flowers and loves them as much as his life." As we were talking, Lan Chang walked over. He smiled and said, "I invited you to appreciate chrysanthemums, not violets. Let's go, let's see the chrysanthemums." He happily led us into the garden. Although the garden was small, it had everything: earthen hills and fish ponds. Hundreds of pots of chrysanthemums of various sizes were arranged around, either leaning against short fences, half-hidden by rocks, emerging from under large tree trunks at an angle, or placed on piles of fallen leaves in the bamboo shade, all containing the composition of a painter according to the plumpness, richness, and lightness of the flowers. Some of the guests were chatting idly on the flower bed lawn, some were standing under the bamboo forest, and some were walking along the winding pebble paths, each according to their own preference. Only the host was busy everywhere, greeting the guests. But my purpose was not to see the chrysanthemums. I invited Lan Chang to sit in a living tree pavilion on the earthen hill. This was a small hexagonal pavilion supported by living trees. Inside, there was a stone table and four wooden benches, directly facing the chrysanthemums. The tree trunks supported the winding railings, making it a great place to sit. At this time, there were a few light clouds like white silk smeared in the sky, and the garden had a new shade, which was very pleasant. Then the treetops shook, making a rustling sound, but a few drops of rain fell. I said, "These few clouds and a few drops of rain are very poetic. It's really a fine rain chrysanthemum day. In this beautiful scene, we must talk about something pleasant. Can Brother Lan's novel material be announced?" Lan Chang smiled and said, "That kind brother hasn't arrived yet." I was stunned and asked, "Which kind brother?" Lan Chang smiled and said, "I said the novel material was hidden in my house, that was wronging you, just to trick you into coming to my house for a meal. As for the supplier of the material, it's a Mr. Ruan. He has quite a bit to do with this matter. Originally, he entrusted me to write a novel. When I inquired about the location of the story, it was Nanjing, Jiujiang, and Beiping. I had no way to describe those three places, so I recommended you. This was also my good intention, because I thought it would be better if the locality in the novel was written more realistically." When I heard Mr. Ruan, I thought of a bearded man. (5)

Three People Walking Together

— Wo Fo

On the way home, I happened to meet three people who were walking in the same direction as me. As we walked along, their appearance and conversation made me realize that these three people were of three different types.

The first was in his thirties, or perhaps not even thirty? Because his face was full of smoker's marks and his skin was so thin that he looked very old. According to what he told the other two, he not only smoked opium but also took red pills. He really looked like his addiction was starting, and his steps seemed so heavy and slack.

The second was quite strong, but his red eyes told of a lack of sleep. He was happily talking about gambling strategies all the way. It is said that he was going to gamble.

The third joined us halfway. He came out of a small hotel, looking very drunk, and an unpleasant smell of alcohol often blew into my nose. After walking a few streets like this, he met a friend, and he pulled this friend into a nearby hotel, saying, "I'll pay the bill."

When I got home, I thought to myself, Confucius said, "When three people walk together, there must be one who can be my teacher." Today I met three people walking together, but which one should I learn from? Smoking, gambling, and drinking are not allowed by Confucius! Then I thought, that's right, these three people are actually my good teachers.

The smoker is constant and persistent, immersed in it, shouldn't I emulate him in my studies? The gambler is brave and persistent, shouldn't I emulate him in my career? The drinker uses drunkenness to relieve sorrow and is generous to friends, shouldn't I emulate him in my interactions with the world? These three people are really my good teachers.

The Grades of Wealthy People

— Shijiu

A and B were equally wealthy, each living in a village, and both were known as wealthy gentlemen. One day, A visited B for something, but B was not home. B's wife knew about it and thought: I've heard that A is also a wealthy person, so I might as well estimate him. I'll go out and entertain him.

When they met, they couldn't help but exchange pleasantries first. Then, A explained the purpose of his visit, so the wealthy lady looked A up and down, making A feel a little embarrassed. Unexpectedly, she suddenly opened her mouth and said, "Looking at you, you're not even a first-class wealthy person, probably second-class!"

A was a little stunned at first, but after calming down, he asked, "May I ask: What's the difference between a first-class wealthy person and a second-class wealthy person?"

Her answer was this: "First-class wealthy people have seven houses, second-class have five houses, and third-class have three houses: this is the standard for determining the grade of wealthy people."

A was even more confused, so he asked, "What do you mean by 'houses'?"

She then answered unhurriedly: "I'll tell you, wealthy people are divided into three grades. Third-grade is just the minimum for a wealthy person. The so-called three houses are: the inner house, the guest house, and the kitchen. Second-grade, when a guest comes, you don't have to open the door yourself, the doorman does it for you; when collecting rent, you don't have to do it yourself, the accountant does it for you. Adding the inner house, the guest house, and the kitchen, isn't that five houses? First-grade, in addition to the five houses, there are also the stable and the concubine's house!"

A was silent for a while before saying, "I'm ashamed to say that I can only be a second-class wealthy person!" It turned out that when A came to visit B, B's wife found out that he had come in a sedan chair, so she said that. On the one hand, it seemed to be mocking A, and on the other hand, it was simply expressing that B was a higher grade than him!

Readers, you can estimate for yourselves which grade you belong to!

New Inventions

Inventions from Around the World

— Jing Renfang

Lightless Cannon During the European War, people invented various methods to observe the location of enemy cannons. These methods generally involved observing the enemy's cannon fire from two locations, and then immediately calculating the true location of the cannon, and using artillery to counterattack. Now, a Dutch inventor has registered a method with the patent office to prevent the enemy from seeing the fire when firing a cannon: that is, when firing a cannon, a stream of liquid mist is sprayed around the muzzle to prevent the heat from coming into contact with the outside air, thus becoming a lightless cannon.

Factory-Style Human Body Model The New York Science Museum recently displayed a human body model whose structure is similar to a factory. Processes like breathing, digestion, blood circulation, and other life activities are shown in a very realistic way. For example, light bulbs are used to represent the flow of carbon dioxide and oxygen, and a grinder represents human molars. The heart is represented by a piston, which allows you to see the movement of blood. Even more interesting is that the brain is divided into areas, and its structure completely follows the natural arrangement of the human brain: 1. Judgment, represented by a court; 2. Intelligence, represented by a classroom; 3. Management, represented by a guide; 4. Muscle control, represented by a railroad switch; 5. Willpower, represented by an executive committee meeting; 6. Breathing management, represented by measuring instruments and scales; 7. Hearing, represented by a recording studio; 8. Vision, represented by a photographer's office; 9. Nerve center, represented by a telephone transformer.

Skyscraper An American architect recently proposed that the government build a 196-story skyscraper in the center of a famous city to serve as a shopping mall, reaching a height of over 2,000 feet. It is said that the construction cost of this shopping mall would be $223 million US. The internal equipment would be sufficient for all commercial applications, and it could accommodate 250,000 people, and could also have large, medium, and small schools, and hospitals and factories, etc. There would also be several floors rented to industrialists as exhibition venues for their products. The construction materials would mainly be steel and white ceramics, and the design would pay attention to art and hygiene.

Heat-Emitting Device Clears Fog Recently, New York City has been testing a heat-emitting device that can clear fog. Once this light is emitted into dense fog, it can be used at airports to allow airplanes to land safely, which is very useful. This device is shaped like a searchlight, but has no lens. It is mounted on a car for easy transfer. The heat emitted is generated by an internal electric arc light. It contains a special electrode, and the current used is the same as that of an ordinary searchlight. The beam of light is very narrow, so its power is very strong, and it can turn water into steam, so it is very easy to reduce fog. When emitted at an airport, the light first sweeps the ground, and then uses mirrors coated with iron foil to reflect it into the sky. Even in heavy fog, a funnel-shaped light can be revealed, and it can soon be completely clear.

Frameless Metal Balloon Recently, the Soviet Union produced a metal balloon with a volume of 1,000 cubic meters that has no frame at all. Its outer shell is made of 0.1 cm thick rust-resistant metal, which is strong and durable. Because there is no rigid frame, the structure can be simplified and economized, and it can be manufactured by machine. The greatest benefit during flight is the elimination of "gas waves," because its outer shell can protect the gas, and it can also use the exhaust gas from the engine. The huge elasticity of the airship allows it to approach the ground for exercises. According to the inventor, the famous scientist Tsiolkovsky, people can manufacture huge airships and become cheap and safe mass transportation tools.

Sports News

Dr. Rong Qizhao in Hong Kong Discusses World Games Football Preselection

Determine player selection with an impartial attitude; The position of football team captain has not yet been decided; Preselection players from various regions are scheduled to depart for Hong Kong

(Hong Kong Correspondent) Dr. Rong Qizhao, a member of the Chinese National Sports Association and the World Games Football Selection Committee, was ordered to come to Hong Kong to preside over everything. He has been in Hong Kong for several days. The day before yesterday, Mr. Rong discussed the arrangements with Yan Chengkun, Chairman of the Hong Kong Sports Association, and others at the Seaview Hotel. Yesterday, reporters interviewed Mr. Rong to inquire about the previous evening's discussion. Mr. Rong absolutely denied the rumors that the official representatives to participate in the World Games football had already been internally decided. Also, good players from both Singapore and Shanghai have telegraphed Hong Kong, and will be arriving soon, expected to be all there before April 4, and the official representatives can be decided on the 12th. There was also discussion about allocating players from Singapore and Shanghai to join the Sanhua First Division for ordinary cup matches. The following is recorded, which is also what those who care about China's participation in the World Games football want to know first.

Problems Arise Along the Way

The reporter first asked Mr. Rong if there were any results from the previous evening's discussion that could be released. According to him, it was just a private conversation that evening, and no concrete discussions were held because the players from various regions had not all arrived. At the same time, there are also problems with the locations of future battles along the way. It is said that the Singapore Football Association is quite unwilling to let its Singaporean players be recruited by China. The proposal to conquer Singapore is currently pending resolution. Also, it is difficult to allocate players from various regions to join the Sanhua team for ordinary cup matches, because the Sanhua teams all have hopes of winning the championship. It will be a problem to assign someone to which team, and even if they are assigned, they may not be able to achieve cooperative effects. Therefore, it is necessary to wait until all the members arrive and see which team needs which players before a proper allocation can be made.

Extremely Cautious about the Qualifications of the Selection Committee

There are a total of five members of the World Games Football Selection Committee, including Shen Siliang as the convener, Hao Gengsheng, Ma John, and Mr. Rong and Yan. According to Mr. Rong, he received a telegram from Shanghai stating that some members of the selection committee, along with players from Shanghai and North China, will depart for Hong Kong by ship today (the 1st) and arrive in three days. Who are the members of the selection committee, and will all three arrive? Because the telegram was brief, it is not yet known in detail and will only be known at the time. As for the qualifications of the selection committee, the Standing Committee of the Association has tried its best to avoid appointing those who are directly related to various parties, such as Mr. Le Xiurong and Yu Hengzhi of Shanghai, and Mr. Huang Jiajun of Hong Kong, all of whom are seniors in the football world, but have not been appointed as selectors for this reason. Among the five selectors, in addition to Yu (Mr. Rong himself) and Yan Shen, Ma Bang has no connection with football. As for the Hong Kong selectors, it is believed that it will be one of Shen and Hao. As for Mr. Ma, it is said that he may not come to participate because Jida University in Beiping does not have a spring break.

Players from Various Regions Arrive in Hong Kong One After Another

Regarding the news of the preliminary players who were originally planned by the National Sports Association to come to Hong Kong to participate in the preselection, the reporter also interviewed Rong Qizhao. According to the answer, now that the preselection period is approaching, many preselection players from various regions are preparing to come to Hong Kong. Yesterday, I received telegrams from North China and East China, and letters from the four Malayan players, reporting their itineraries. Players from North China, such as Tan Fuzhen, have arrived in Shanghai and decided to join players from East China and take the President McKinley south tomorrow (the 1st), arriving in Hong Kong in about three days. The original plan was for everyone to take the Java ship, but it would not arrive until the 5th. I saw that the 4th and 5th were Saturdays and Sundays, and there were football matches in Hong Kong, so I telegraphed everyone to rush to Hong Kong to participate. As for the four Malayan players, Cai Wenli, Xie Fuqing, Liang Li'an, and Lin Ziquan, they also wrote to report that they will take the Jinma to Hong Kong to participate in the preselection competition. As for Li Yuxin from Java, there is still no news, and I don't know if he will be able to come to Hong Kong. Even if he doesn't come, it won't have any impact.

The Football Captain Has Not Yet Been Decided

Then the reporter asked, "It was previously reported that the foreign specialist football team has decided to appoint Li Huitang as the captain. Is this true?" Mr. Rong replied with a smile, "Regarding this point, I dare to say that the captain has not been decided. In the future, Li may be appointed, but this is not something I dare to decide in advance. Because the official team has not yet been selected, how can there be a captain? Even Mr. Li himself is only a selected player at present. And I dare to be responsible for telling you that this time the National Sports Association is selecting players in an absolutely open manner, not as rumored outside, that it has already been decided. Please think about it, the five selection committee members appointed by the Association, Ma John, Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, Yan Chengkun, and myself, are all neutral and have no private relationship with any players, so in the future, they will definitely act impartially."

Selecting Players Impartially

Finally, the reporter asked Mr. Rong, "Did you watch the International Cup football match on Sunday?" Mr. Rong replied, "Yes." Asked, "Did the players perform well?" Replied, "Everyone was excellent." Asked, "The Hong Kong Chinese and Western newspapers said that right winger Deng Guangsen was one of the best players that day. How do you feel?" Replied, "His performance was indeed good that day." Regarding the question of selected players, in addition to the 30 players on the list, do others who have made progress also have a chance of being selected? Replied, "It is natural to be selected, because the official representatives will only select 22 people, and 10 or 8 people will need to be eliminated from the 30 people. However, in any case, the Association will definitely act impartially based on the second method of selection."

Shanghai Municipal Art Education Promotion Association Sends Telegram to the Ministry of Education to Withdraw its Order, and Schedules a General Meeting for the 18th

After the promulgation of the revised curriculum standards, art educators in this city specially organized the Art Education Promotion Association and held a committee meeting the day before yesterday. The chairman was Zhao Weizu, and the recorder was Zhu Zhiwei. Zhu Zhiwei was elected to draft a telegram to the Ministry of Education to withdraw its order, and a letter was sent to art teachers in primary and secondary schools in this city to solicit participation. A general meeting was scheduled to be convened on the 18th of this month to discuss the next steps. The original telegram is as follows: (omitted above) According to reports, the revised curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools will reduce the teaching time for subjects such as drawing, music, and manual labor. This may be the result of a temporary proposal by a few people without in-depth exploration. As far as I can see, I think it is inappropriate. The purpose of subjects such as art is to cultivate the body and mind and enlighten the spirit, which is closely related to moral, intellectual, and physical education. Whether we emphasize vocational education or production education, we must not neglect them. Moreover, any career must have a fulfilling life before it can be pursued. How can we make life fulfilling? It is impossible without art. Some say that the society is in a slump, foreign aggression is imminent, and the people will be uneasy and the country will be insecure. The only way to save the situation is to promote science. Therefore, the art curriculum is greatly reduced. I also think it is not right. Any discipline must have sufficient creativity and thinking ability before it can make progress and make inventions. How can we develop creativity and enhance thinking ability? It is impossible without art. Therefore, some provinces advocate art education, and education experts have researched and believe that the teaching hours of subjects such as art should not be less than one-fifth of the total. These are the results of decades of educational experience and dozens of thorough and careful explorations. The importance of subjects such as art can be generally seen. Now, the Ministry has a unique proposal to reduce them. I don't know what it is based on. It is really puzzling. Perhaps it is because it has been nearly thirty years since our country increased art education, and the achievements obtained are minimal, and the effectiveness of the art education curriculum is small, so it is based on this that there is a proposal to reduce it. It is not known that the promotion of art education in our country in the past was all empty words. There was only its appearance, and most of the school authorities also violated it secretly and reduced it privately. It is naturally not easy to seek satisfactory achievements in this way. The shortcomings of the past are there, not here. The Ministry should deeply investigate its source and seek ways to remedy it. If another order is issued to reduce it, it will be a loss of the original intention of promotion. The colleagues of this association are in their duties and dare not remain silent. We hereby send a telegram to your seat, and we urge you to withdraw your order and maintain the original teaching hours of drawing, music, and manual labor subjects in primary and secondary schools. We also ask you to order all primary and secondary schools in the country to implement them in accordance with the standards, and must not neglect them, so as not to make the students feel spiritually flawed, and the future of culture will be greatly affected. Education is fortunate, the nation is fortunate.

School Survey

Overview of the French School in Shanghai (4)

By Hu Zuyin

The advantages and disadvantages of this strict training can also be explained. First, the main purpose of French education is to cultivate the intellectual development of students as much as possible; therefore, less attention is paid to physical training and social education. However, this extremely training can enable French schools to maintain higher academic standards, which is not the case in schools in other countries. First, after French children have undergone strict training in primary and secondary schools, they will inevitably abuse this freedom when they enjoy individual freedom in college. Fortunately, French children have acquired a habit of engaging in normal and efficient intellectual work in primary and secondary schools, which can balance the tendency to abuse freedom. Third, after French children have undergone this strict training in primary and secondary schools, they can become citizens of the French democratic country when they reach adulthood.

In the French school in Shanghai, there is also a special training, which is to cultivate children with a spirit of international harmony. Although there are children of 26 nationalities in the school, the children of various countries do not have an attitude of mutual hostility or contempt in their daily interactions. According to Mr. Gao Boai, he has been the director of the school for more than 20 years (Editor's note: Mr. Gao was originally the principal of the school. Now, because the school business of the French Municipal Council is heavy, a new education department has recently been established, and Mr. Gao has been transferred to the director of the education department. He often instructs the students of the school that there should be no racial or national prejudices among the students. The training of the elected international spirit has now achieved considerable success, which is something that Mr. Gao is proud of.

5. Freedom of Thought

Although French schools strictly supervise the behavior of students, they absolutely respect the freedom of thought of students. This freedom of thought can not only be enjoyed by French college students, but also by French primary and secondary schools. The methods of cultivating freedom of thought are carried out in two aspects: teachers and students. In terms of teachers, no teacher may promote any political party, ideology, or religious opinion in the classroom. Schools may not support a certain party, exclude a certain faction; persuade to believe in a certain doctrine, attack other doctrines; do not promote religion, nor oppose religion. In short, schools absolutely respect freedom of thought and belief.

In terms of students, students are free to express their personal thoughts and beliefs. However, his expressions must be rational and biased towards research, not blindly supporting or excluding a certain party or doctrine. Teachers can of course try their best to revise students' homework and articles, but they should try their best to preserve students' pure rational and research-oriented thoughts and beliefs, and should not add or delete them based on personal preferences.

Commercial News

Finance Bank Selling Pressure Intensifies Gold Price Selling Climaxes —Result: Down $1.20—

Yesterday's gold market saw rumors of cash exports and the debunking of a bubble. Buyers adopted a wait-and-see approach, and banks engaged in selling, leading to a surge in selling pressure and a downward trend. Initial selling caused a slight fluctuation in forward silver prices in the Montreux area, rising by 1.5 li and then falling by 2.5 li. Exchange rates remained stable. London spot gold fell by 0.5 pence. The Central Bank's posted rates were unchanged for both British and American currencies, and the customs gold unit remained stable. The gold standard price was lowered to $1143.20. The preliminary trading session opened around $46.00, slightly lower than the morning. After the opening, major sellers continued to sell, pushing prices down. However, buying activity emerged at the lower prices, leading to a slight rebound. The HSBC's posted rates revealed no change for British and American currencies, resulting in a stable situation. The silver balance tax decreased by 0.5%. Subsequently, major sellers aggressively sold bars, and the market lacked support. Bank selling pressure intensified, gradually driving prices lower. Later, buying interest from dual accounts increased, with rumors of a certain bank selling bars, dampening market sentiment and causing a temporary decline. However, after reaching the low, major buyers emerged to compete for purchases, stabilizing the market by noon. In the afternoon, the market opened slightly lower, but major buyers jointly purchased bars, gradually showing signs of recovery. Although some took profits at higher prices, initial reports of Indian silver were small, and the second report was unchanged. Buying interest remained strong, stabilizing the market. Tight Lending is Not the Solution

This year, the silver and money industry remains exceptionally cautious regarding credit lending to various commercial firms. Aside from selectively lending to long-standing customers from last year, new accounts are largely rejected. According to current surveys, each money house has opened no more than three or four hundred accounts, mostly with frequent transactions, largely adhering to a tight credit policy. However, about ten firms, including Fuyuan, Shun Kang, Dunyu, Tongyu, Chengyu, Ankang, Jintai, Cunde, and Wufeng, can be considered exceptions. Therefore, in this year's general commerce, although cash is not available for goods purchases, a ten-day note is often required as compensation; otherwise, the deal will be rejected. As the deadline for the quarterly settlement approaches, efforts should be made to remedy this situation.

Wuyuan Tea Industry Also Knows Improvement

In recent years, the Wuyuan tea industry has been declining due to the sluggish sales of Russian farms. The main reason is that the harvesting period of Wuyuan green tea is near the beginning of summer, which leads to coarse branches and large leaves, with more old grass and fewer tender tips. Now the Russian route is completely hopeless, and this coarse-leaf tribute green tea is not sold. However, ignorant tea households still do not pick tender leaves early. It is understood that the Wuyuan Tea Industry Association deeply feels that if the green tea in this area is not actively improved, it will inevitably be naturally eliminated. It is heard that they have formally established an improvement agency and are striving to improve the various methods of technology and baking. In particular, they believe that early picking of tender leaves is the key to survival. In addition to sending personnel to various villages to spread the word, they also plan to petition the government to strictly prohibit the sale of old tea.

Anhui Tea Research (1)

— Shi Jifa

(1) Tea Producing Areas, Types, and Output in Anhui Province

Anhui is rich in products, with tea being the most prominent. Its soil is fertile, and its processing is excellent, so it is sold throughout the country and exported to Europe, America, and Southeast Asia, all with high praise. Although other provinces in China, such as Fujian, Zhejiang, Hunan, Jiangxi, Hubei, also produce tea, they cannot compare. Anhui is the richest tea-producing area, with almost every county north and south of the Yangtze River producing tea. Tea produced north of the river is collectively called "North Tea." Tea produced south of the river is collectively called "South Tea." The green tea produced in Lu'an and Huoshan counties in northern Anhui is famous throughout the country, while the black tea produced in Qiupu (Zhizhi) and Qimen in southern Anhui is renowned overseas. The so-called "Hui-Lu'an Famous Tea" has a long history. Researching its historical origins, green tea began in the Wei and Jin Dynasties and flourished in the Tang and Song Dynasties. The tea industry began in Qiupu. Thirty-seven years before the founding of the Republic of China, a man named Yu from Yi County opened a black tea factory in Yaodu Street, Qiupu County, to test the production of black tea. The following year, he went to Qimen to set up a branch factory, encouraging tea farmers to use fermentation and other methods. In the third year, he opened a black tea factory in the western district of Qimen. At the same time, Hu Yeru, a wealthy tea farmer in the southern district of Qimen, specially made garden tea to promote it. This was the beginning of the conversion of Anhui tea to black tea. Since then, the number of black tea factories has increased year by year, and Qiupu and Dingzi counties have become areas in Anhui Province that produce black tea.

Anhui has a vast tea-producing area and a very rich output, with more than twenty counties involved. The province's tea-producing areas are now divided into five categories as follows:

Various counties under Huizhou Prefecture: Huizhou was formerly a prefecture in Anhui Province. The six counties are located in southern Anhui, bordering western Jiangxi, western Zhejiang, and the Shapai River. The area is mostly mountainous, with little plains, so agricultural products are centered around tea. In the past, transportation was via the Xin'an River and the upper reaches of the Chang River and Leping River, with Tunxi and Wuyuan (now under the jurisdiction of Jiangxi Province) serving as hubs for the concentration of grains and tea leaves. Wuyuan, Dingzi, Qimen, Xiuning, and She County produce the most tea, and their quality is the best in Anhui. Both red and green tea are available. Yi County's Xuxi also produces more than one million dan per year. In total, Huizhou's annual tea output accounts for a large proportion of China's tea exports. Among them, the black tea produced in Qimen is mostly concentrated in the inland areas of Jiangxi Province. Other areas mostly produce green tea, with Wuyuan producing the most, accounting for half of Huizhou's green tea. Therefore, Huizhou tea is also known as Wuyuan tea, and because it is concentrated in Tunxi, it is also known as Tunxi tea. Xiuning and She County produce the second most, and Yi County's Xuxi produces less. In addition to being exported by foreign firms, Anhui tea is also sold in Jiangsu, Shandong, Jiangxi, Hubei, Guangdong, Beijing, Shanghai, Tianjin, Wuhan, and other provinces and cities.

Jiande and Qingyang counties in Chizhou: Both Qingyang and Jiande counties in Chizhou are under the jurisdiction of the old Chizhou Prefecture in southern Anhui. They also produce tea, but the quality is inferior to that produced in Huizhou, and the output is not much. In addition to self-sufficiency, very little is exported. It is not often seen in Beijing and Shanghai, but it can also be found in Fuzhou and Wuhan markets.

Lu'an's Yingshan, Huoshan, Shucheng, and Huoqiu counties: All belong to northern Anhui, and they are known for their scented green tea, such as Jin Chun and Jiang. This kind of tea is mostly sold in the Shanghai market, followed by Wuhan, and also in Fuzhou. A large amount is also sold to foreign firms, with an annual output of no less than hundreds of thousands of boxes. Lu'an is one of the tea distribution centers in northern Anhui. Every tea season, many Shandong merchants come to the market with handcarts, stay in tea shops, and purchase large quantities of tea, which they resell in Shandong via intermediate routes. (The tea season is from late April to early May).

Fengyang and Shouzhou counties: Also belong to northern Anhui, and both produce tea. The tea produced in Shouzhou is called Shouchun tea, which is excellent. Many Shanghai people use it because of its fragrant taste. (To be continued)

Page 15

Shen Bao Medical Special

Red Eggs

— Yao XingShu

— Here's Why You Might Not Get to Eat Them —

Chicken eggs, duck eggs, preserved eggs, Gaoyou salted duck eggs, spiced tea eggs—gentlemen with plenty of legal tender in their wallets can always buy and eat them. But red eggs are different. Unless "my precious" has just been born, they're not easy to come by. It's truly a case of "searching high and low without success, then getting them without any effort."

Society's custom is that only when someone has a son or daughter do they feel overjoyed and send red eggs to relatives and friends. Only then do others get to eat red eggs. Hence, "When are we eating red eggs?" has become a humorous catchphrase circulating in society.

It is said that my Lord Jesus had no father. His mother, Mary, conceived through the Holy Spirit of God and gave birth to Jesus. Who is God? What is the Holy Spirit? I am a humble scholar and dare not offer reckless opinions, so I'll leave that aside. Modern knowledge tells us that to have children, a man and a woman must cooperate intimately. However, there are many men and women who live together for a long time but cannot conceive. When they will eat red eggs is utterly unknown, truly causing people to long with aching eyes.

Regarding the issue of fertility, I, an astrologer, have done much research. Whether one can conceive or not can be known on the spot simply by charting a woman's birth data and predicting a man's yearly luck. Whether it's accurate to speak of the past and predict the future, you'll know on the spot if it's accurate, and you'll know afterwards if it's effective. "You have no descendants... At twenty, childless, you laugh merrily; at thirty, childless, you hang your head low." The reason for infertility is very simple: "It's fate, it's luck, what more can be said?"

"Medicine," "divination," "astrology," and "physiognomy" have been known as top-tier professions since ancient times. I humbly acknowledge my ignorance, having only learned "medicine." I'm a complete layman when it comes to the study of fate, a total simpleton who doesn't understand. However, although I'm a poor doctor, I've always been keen on pursuing principles. The reasons for infertility, from a medical perspective, require much investigation. Readers are all clever friends, so let's see, who's right? Who's wrong?

Before getting to the main topic, I must first speak up for young women.

China is a male-centered society, where women are always at a disadvantage—no, that's not entirely true now—and infertility is also blamed on women. In reality, women are only half responsible for fertility. If a woman and a man live together for years without conceiving, she is immediately labeled an infertile stone woman, which in ancient times was grounds for divorce. Now, although the law doesn't allow it, men still use the excuse of taking a concubine to prepare for passing on the family line, which is perfectly justifiable. This is truly killing people! Those innocent, abandoned women, how wronged! How wronged! You must know that not all men are all-powerful in fertility. Even if an infertile man takes hundreds of concubines, it won't do any good.

In short, to have sons and daughters, there must be sexual intercourse, and sperm must unite with an egg. If either of these processes is obstructed, then no matter how much you burn incense day and night or worship Buddha, even sincerity won't work. Now, I will explain the medical causes of infertility below for your consideration.

(A) Inability to have intercourse

If a man's penis has congenital abnormalities, is abnormally small or excessively large, or is partially damaged due to external injuries or various diseases (including venereal diseases), or is surgically removed, or has scar-induced contractions, or due to surrounding diseases such as inguinal hernias, hydroceles, elephantiasis, etc., the penis may be able to erect or barely erect, but due to one of the above-mentioned obstacles, it cannot achieve its purpose. In medicine, this is called organic disorder of the penis.

Organic disorders of the penis always have clues that can be found; but the functional disorders of the penis that I'm talking about here are different. Outwardly, they look impressive, but they are weak and incompetent, unable to erect, or the erection is weak. These symptoms are seen in patients with neurasthenia, diseases of the brain and spinal cord, excessive debauchery and masturbation, and sexual perversion. These so-called impotent men can only sigh in vain before being cured.

The female vagina is used to accommodate the penis and receive its ejaculated semen. If this part undergoes changes, congenital or acquired abnormalities, such as vaginal closure, narrow vaginal opening, fused labia, tough hymen, scar-induced vaginal constriction, if this path is blocked, it will cause obstruction. This is called organic vaginal atrophy in women. In addition, although the structure of the vagina has not changed at all, many women with mental disorders and hypersensitivity, as soon as the penis approaches the private parts, the vagina immediately experiences high spasms, resulting in the male being unable to ejaculate. There is also a type of woman who, due to various environmental factors, is usually depressed and unhappy, indifferent to human affairs, and has extremely weak sexual desire. The secretion of the cervical canal glands is scarce, and the sperm ejaculated by the man cannot survive for long in the acidic vaginal fluid, losing the opportunity to unite with the egg. Although "that" has happened, it is still not easy to conceive. This is called psychogenic vaginal atrophy in women.

(B) Narrowly defined infertility

A man's only reproductive ability is sperm, which is produced in the testicles. If the testicles are diseased, do not produce sperm, or the sperm has lost its vitality in the testicles, or the sperm cannot be discharged due to blockage of the passage, etc., then one cannot have children, but the matter of sexual intercourse can still be done hard and practically.

Congenital absence of testicles is a type of malformation. Because it cannot produce sperm, it is absolutely impossible to have children. If one side is missing, there is still hope for fertility.

If the testicles do not descend into the scrotum but remain hidden in the abdomen or inguinal canal, they cannot fully develop, the tissues atrophy, and they cannot produce sperm.

If the testicles are removed or exposed to X-rays, they lose the ability to produce sperm.

The testicles atrophy and their function degenerates due to masturbation and excessive sexual activity, orchitis, epididymitis (mostly caused by gonorrhea), etc.

Testicular syphilis, tuberculosis, tumors, etc., cause the function to disappear.

Lack of sperm.

Semen (in which sperm float) is obstructed from being discharged due to foreskin, vas deferens scar contraction, tumor compression of the vas deferens, etc.

(C) Female inability to conceive

In this item, the male bears no responsibility. Conception requires the union of a female egg and sperm. If a woman's ovaries do not produce eggs, the fallopian tubes are blocked due to disease, there is a congenital lack of ovaries, or there are diseases of the ovaries themselves, as well as diseases of the uterus, etc., the site of egg production, the path it passes through, and the incubator for the embryo have changed, so naturally conception cannot occur.

Judging from the above, there are many reasons for infertility. Which side, male or female, should bear more responsibility? The statistics from various sources are inconsistent, but it doesn't matter, so I'll skip it. It's not to please women or speak up for them, but they may not bear more responsibility for infertility.

A Global View of Tuberculosis Statistics (4)

— Ding HuiKang

The mortality statistics for countries in North America vary greatly. For example, a 1926 report from New York State showed a difference of 1.48 to 50.0 deaths per 10,000 residents. It is difficult to study such differences. Michigan, located in the central part of the northern United States, had fewer tuberculosis deaths between 1901 and 1926 than the southern states, but Michigan's population is very dense. This decrease may be due to the influence of foreign residents or the presence of many sanatoriums in the south. In general, the greatest reasons for the decrease in tuberculosis deaths are the development of industry, the improvement of living standards, and the efforts of tuberculosis prevention. According to Green's report, in Cleveland, there were 14.6 deaths in 1910 (per 10,000 residents), but only 8.3 deaths in 1930 (per 10,000 residents). People of color, whose living standards have not been fully improved, do not seem to be able to achieve this reduction in tuberculosis deaths.

In Mexico, tuberculosis mortality has also decreased in recent years. Although Mexico City often has various unfortunate incidents, in 1900 there were 50.0 deaths per 10,000 residents, but in 1929 it had decreased to 13.0 deaths. Funding for tuberculosis prevention comes mostly from charitable donations.

In South America, Argentina and Brazil reported tuberculosis deaths in 1926, and the mortality rate was still very high due to poor public health. The Philippines has a 30-year history of tuberculosis prevention, but it has not yet achieved its goals. In 1926, there were 29.27 deaths per 10,000 residents, 28.76 deaths in 1928, and 30.55 deaths in 1930. In 1904, 18.43% of cattle had a positive tuberculin reaction.

The situation in Japan and China is similar to the above. However, it should be noted that the mortality rates in each region are different. According to Mr. Peng, there are fewer cases of tuberculosis in northern and western China, and more transmission in central and southern China. China's tuberculosis prevention facilities were first initiated in 1913. Mayor Wu and others recently initiated the China Tuberculosis Prevention Association, which has now established several clinics. Detailed work reports should be available soon to satisfy readers' desires, so I will not repeat them here.

In San Francisco, USA, the mortality rate among Chinese and Japanese residents is 45.9 per 10,000 people, while among other ethnic groups it is only 9.93 per 10,000 people. These observations are quite surprising, as the aggressiveness of tuberculosis seems to vary among different ethnic groups.

When discussing tuberculosis from the perspective of race, special attention must be paid to the place of growth. For example, the tuberculosis mortality rate among blacks and Indians in Canada, the United States, and Mexico is generally extremely high, while the mortality rate among whites in the same location is much lower. In addition, the mixing of blood, i.e., interracial marriage, may increase resistance and reduce tuberculosis mortality, but it does not reduce its contagiousness. Mr. Grouch has definitely proven that between 1926 and 1930, there were 132.7 deaths per 10,000 residents among Indians, while there were only 33.9 deaths among whites. Most interestingly, one-third of all Indian deaths occurred around the age of fifteen. In addition, Mantoux's tuberculin test was 75% positive in Indian children, 34 to 39% in mixed-race children, and 22.6% in white children. The high rate of infection among these Indians is clearly due to poor hygiene.

Common Knowledge Q&A About Diseases

— Cheng HanZhang

(80) Pernicious Anemia

What is Pernicious Anemia?

This is an independent type of anemia. The disease progresses continuously; it is not caused by external influences such as blood loss, poisoning, or inappropriate lifestyle.

What are the causes of pernicious anemia?

Page 16

There are many causes of pernicious anemia. The main ones are toxic effects in the blood or hematopoietic tissues, or poor hematopoietic function in the body itself. Other causes include tapeworm infestation, syphilis, pregnancy, etc., but generally it is due to toxic effects.

Is the occurrence of pernicious anemia related to age?

Pernicious anemia occurs more often in middle age (35 to 50 years old) and later. But it sometimes occurs in adolescents as well.

Is pernicious anemia related to gender?

It is more common in women.

What are the initial symptoms of this type of anemia?

The onset of pernicious anemia is insidious, so it is impossible to know when it started. But in the beginning, the patient feels tired, muscle fatigue, headache, dizziness, tinnitus, increased heart palpitations, loss of appetite, nausea, pale skin and mucous membranes, sometimes burning sensation on the tongue, diarrhea, lack of gastric acid, and neurological symptoms.

What symptoms develop later?

Later symptoms include pale skin and mucous membranes, retinal hemorrhage, or optic neuritis, rapid breathing, increased heart rate, anemic heart murmurs, digestive disorders, belching, lack of appetite, constipation, enlarged spleen, dark brown urine, sometimes containing protein, and often mixed with urobilinogen. There is an abnormal sensation in the hands and feet, lower limb ataxia, increased tendon reflexes, and the body temperature rises slightly every afternoon. The mucous membranes of various parts are prone to bleeding.

What changes occur in the blood of patients with pernicious anemia?

The blood is pale, watery, slow to coagulate, and the serum is dark yellow. The number of red blood cells is reduced, with only 1.5 million or even less than 1 million per cubic millimeter. Hemoglobin is also reduced. White blood cells are fewer than normal, and lymphocytes are increased.

How long does pernicious anemia last, and what is the prognosis?

It lasts for a long time, from six months to a year, or even more slowly, up to ten years or more. The disease is severe, and if not treated properly, it is difficult to avoid death.

What is the treatment for pernicious anemia?

A relatively new method for treating pernicious anemia is liver therapy, which involves eating animal liver or liver preparations every day, and injecting liver preparations such as Campolon, Livex, and Hepracton. The second is to inject arsenic preparations and take Asiatic pills and Arcylen pills internally. In addition, blood transfusion therapy is performed, and digestive agents such as dilute hydrochloric acid and pepsin are taken internally for poor appetite. Non-specific stimulation therapy, such as the injection of casein and milk preparations, can also be tried. Some people advocate splenectomy, but this cannot be done. (End)

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued)

— Zhou MengBai

Platycodaceae

(1) Balloon Flower Platycodon grandiflorum, DC.

"Plant" Grows wild in the wilderness and can also be cultivated. It is a perennial herb. The stem is 60-90 cm tall. The leaves are alternate, petiolate, lanceolate or oblong, with serrated edges. In summer and autumn, it blooms with purple or white five-lobed bell-shaped flowers. The capsule is spherical.

"Cultivation Method" Sow in seedbeds in spring, and transplant to the main field in late autumn. For layering, space the rows two feet apart and each plant six inches apart. The following spring, when new shoots grow to about one foot tall, add soil to the base of the roots to prevent lodging. Use human manure and oil cake as fertilizer. The harvesting period is from November of the fifth year after sowing to March of the following year. When harvesting, dig up the roots, remove the stems, wash off the dirt, and dry them in the sun. Each mu can yield about 370 catties of fresh roots. Autumn roots are best for drying Balloon Flower.

"Crude Drug" Balloon Flower Root Radix Platycodonis is collected from the roots and dried. The product is spindle-shaped, 10-15 cm long, 3 cm thick, curved and branched, and uneven in size. The surface has longitudinal deep wrinkles, similar to yellowish-brown, and the texture is rough. The fracture surface is fibrous, white or light yellow. The taste is bitter.

The cross-section of the root is irregular in shape. The outer periphery, with a curved outer layer, is covered with a dark brown tegument. The inside is white. The thick part of the bark is roughly the same as that of the wood. There are cracks everywhere. The cambium is along the brown ring money. The sieve tube and vascular bundle are in the shape of brown radial lines.

Examining the cross-section under a microscope, the bark is purely composed of parenchyma tissue, with stone cell nuclei, but no mixed fibers. In the secondary bark, there are multiple latex tubes, and the vascular bundles are arranged in a row.

Dried Balloon Flower is the root that has been peeled of its tegument and dried. The surface is similar to white, and the texture is light.

"Ingredients" The roots contain Kikyosaponin C29H48O11. When this Saponin is mixed and boiled with acid, it is hydrolyzed as follows: C29H48O11+H2O=C23H38O6+C6 (Galactose)

Japanese scholars such as Mr. UmeTsuji and Mr. Ohluka have done considerable research on the Saponin of this plant.

"Pharmacology" The Balloon Flower Saponin obtained by Mr. UmeTsuji exhibits complete hemolysis in a 10,000-fold solution. The Balloon Flower Saponin obtained by Mr. Ohluka is even more potent than the former. The lethal dose of Balloon Flower Saponin for mice is 7.7 mg of subcutaneous injection for mice weighing 10 cm.

"Medicinal Use" Old sayings: Balloon Flower root is used as an expectorant and for throat diseases. The daily dose is 8 grams, used as a decoction, but licorice is often added.

Prescription Example: Balloon Flower Decoction, has the effect of expectorant and cough suppressant.

Balloon Flower 4.0 Licorice 8.0

The above is a decoction of 200, taken in three divided doses a day.

New Drugs: New drugs made from Balloon Flower root are as follows.

Platycodin (Balloon Flower Root Fluid Extract.)

Hustol (a cough suppressant, which contains ephedra.)

Evanin

Hygiene Knowledge of Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Diseases (Continued)

— Tang RenJin

(84) Vitreous Opacity

The vitreous body is a colorless, transparent, gelatinous substance. It is in the posterior part of the eyeball. It fills the vitreous cavity surrounded by the lens, ciliary body, and retina. Its shape. Is slightly spherical. It also has refractive power. The front is connected to the lens. The contact part is concave in the shape of a dish. The vitreous body itself has no inherent nerves or blood vessels. Its nutrition is supplied by the adjacent uvea. Therefore, the vitreous body is also often affected in diseases of the inner eye membranes, such as retinitis, choroiditis, and ciliary body inflammation.

Speaking of the causes of vitreous opacity. Most are caused by syphilitic or tuberculous uveitis or retinochoroiditis. Others occur after acute infectious diseases, severe myopia, retinal detachment, and vitreous hemorrhage. The degree of opacity is not the same. Some exist throughout the vitreous body, some are localized to the anterior or posterior part, or some are scattered individually. The shape of the opacity varies. Fine ones are like dust. Slightly larger ones are like dots, flakes, filaments, plaques, and membranes. These opacities often cause visual impairment in patients. When the patient's eyeball moves. There are dark spots floating in the field of vision. Like mosquitoes flying in the evening in summer. This is what is called floaters. If we use transillumination to examine. Most are easily seen to be opaque. In the red pupil collar. There are black or grayish-white opaque or translucent dust, dots, flakes, filaments, plaques, membranes, and other opaque substances. If the patient moves the eyeball up and down or left and right. Then the opacity can be seen floating in the eye. If combined with vitreous liquefaction. Then the movement of the eyeball is not necessary. It is also possible to observe the floating of opaque objects.

The first thing to do in this disease is to treat the underlying disease. Try absorbent and conduction therapy. Pay attention to the state of systemic nutrition. If it is syphilitic, it is especially suitable to implement anti-syphilis therapy.

Furthermore, when healthy eyes are staring at a white wall or the sky. Often there are translucent droplet-like, flocculent, or filamentous dark spots. This is because of the cells and connective tissue fibers remaining in the vitreous body during the fetal period. In medicine, it is specifically called physiological vitreous opacity. Moderate myopia is more likely to occur. There are four characteristics of this opacity: 　The number of dark spots is approximately constant and does not often increase. 　The dark spots are mostly fixed and do not move, but when the eyeball moves, they also move with it. 　The patient's vision is not impaired. And 　If examined by transillumination, it is often impossible to prove the opacity.

Physiological vitreous opacity often does not require treatment.

Tooth Knowledge Q&A (27)

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 132) Why should mouthwash be selected and prepared by a doctor?

Answer: Because everyone's oral condition is different, and special oral conditions should use special mouthwash. For example, people with excessive acidity in their mouths are prone to tooth decay and should use more alkaline medicines to neutralize the acidity. If there is too much alkalinity in the saliva, tartar accumulates, and it is easy to develop periodontal disease, then alkaline medicines should not be used too much. Generally speaking, most people suffer from acidity in their mouths.

(Question 133) The mouthwashes sold on the market are mostly expensive. Are there any cheap and good mouthwashes that can be prepared and used regularly?

Answer: There are two types: The first is lime water. Just buy dozens of coins worth of quicklime, dissolve it in water, let it release heat and settle, filter out the clear water on top, and store it in a bottle. Or store the water and the settled lime at the bottom together in a container. After the water on top is almost used up, add water again. This way, you can always have a saturated amount of lime water to use. When using lime water to rinse your mouth, you can add some warm water to avoid the taste being too strong. The second type is physiological saline, or 1% saline. When preparing it, just use one part salt and 100 parts boiling water. These two types are indeed the easiest to prepare, the most economical, and the best mouthwashes. Families should keep them on hand and use them from time to time. If saline is mixed with a small amount of lime water, the effect will be even better. Lime water can also be added to milk for children to drink, which can help with milk digestion.

(Question 134) How should people with excessive acidity in their mouths protect their teeth?

Answer: People with abnormal saliva and excessive acidity in their mouths are prone to tooth decay and are extremely sensitive. Local relief seeks to neutralize the acidity in the mouth. The following drugs can be used:

(1) Baking soda: Use a small spoonful of baking soda and mix it with a teacup of boiling water. Rinse your mouth often, once after meals and before going to bed.

(2) Lime water: As mentioned above, it can be used for regular mouthwash.

(3) Milk of magnesia: Use it after brushing your teeth, at least once every night before going to bed. Take a spoonful of milk of magnesia, pour it into your mouth, and use the movement of your tongue and cheeks to spread it on the surface of your teeth. This method is very effective.

(4) Tooth powder made of calcium carbonate or magnesium carbonate also has the effect of neutralizing acidity.

(Question 135) What are the harms of tartar?

Answer: The nature of tartar has already been discussed in questions 88 and 89 above. It has many harms. First, it can irritate the gums, gradually causing redness, swelling, and inflammation, easily leading to bleeding and even suppuration, becoming periodontal disease. Second, it is the main base for oral bacteria to reside, causing tooth decay, stomatitis, and a breeding ground for pharyngitis. Third, it accumulates thicker and thicker, the gums recede due to pressure, and the roots of the teeth are exposed, making them prone to looseness. Fourth, it can damage the aesthetics of the teeth, covering the white teeth with various dirty colors.
