Blessing and Curse

— Meng Ruo

The Bishop of St. Paul's Cathedral in London held a grand public prayer meeting the night before last to bless those in various countries who bear the heavy responsibility of the current situation. King Edward VIII of England and his staff, French President Lebrun and other cabinet members, German leader Hitler, and other important administrative officials of various countries were all named. However, it is heard that this is the first time that Mr. Xi has been included in the public prayer of the English church.

Recently, the situation in Europe has been turbulent, causing people to be panicked and fear the impending disaster. Therefore, churches in various countries often pray for peace, hoping that the merciful God can have mercy on the suffering of the people and turn misfortune into blessing for the world. The year before last, when the Chaco War between America and Bolivia was in full swing, on the Savior's birth day, the church appealed to both sides to cease fire for one day, so that the warriors on the battlefield could also receive the Lord's blessing and rest. On the same day last year, when Italy and Ethiopia were confronting each other in East Africa, the church made the same request. Once, the Pope of Rome even held a large peace prayer meeting, ordering Catholics around the world to pray continuously for three days. This is a manifestation of the charitable spirit of Catholics. Unfortunately, no matter how much they pray, human catastrophe is still unavoidable. The great war in East Africa killed and injured countless lives. This is probably the will of heaven, which cannot be saved by human power. Otherwise, the prayers of Catholics must be sincere and devout.

This time, the Bishop of St. Paul's Cathedral in England probably saw the ineffectiveness of previous peace prayers, so he changed his approach and blessed the current political leaders of Europe. This intention is also very good. Those important officials who are prayed for happen to be in this great era, bearing the heavy responsibility of the current situation. It is really too hard, and they should be prayed for, begging God to bless them all with good health so that they can seek peace and tranquility for mankind. Mr. Xi has never been included in the public prayer of the English church. This time, I think it is because he is considered to be pivotal to the European situation, so he is also blessed once.

However, the attitude of ordinary people is different from that of Catholics. They often utter curses against some political leaders in various countries around the world. The reason is that these big figures mostly have a kind of ambition. On the surface, they never tire of saying that they love peace, but in reality, they are all scheming against each other, preparing to slaughter. They yearn to achieve a heroic career under their own iron fist. The turmoil in the world today is all caused by them. And the fate of mankind is held in their hands, at their disposal. They are so headstrong, taking their own will as their will, so naturally everyone will not have any good feelings towards them.

"Chaotian Restaurant"

— Guo Ka

——Travel Notes

It started snowing when the car left Jinan. Pressing my forehead against the cold glass, I looked out the window. The flickering electric lights gradually disappeared, and my eyes were filled with a vague wilderness. The light in the car quickly brushed past the slopes by the roadside through the window, and the ground gradually turned white. In the light and shadow outside the window, there were also snowflakes shaking and flashing, or tiredly sticking to the window glass, turning into water droplets and flowing down in curves.

I turned around in disappointment and let out a light sigh into the carriage, where most of the passengers were already asleep. The journey of the past few days, suddenly encountering such snowy weather, made me feel a little apprehensive about the journey tomorrow.

After midnight, in a burst of commotion, I opened my eyes from my sleep. Someone on the platform outside was shaking a bell and shouting in a hoarse voice:

"Weixian Weixian..."

I groggily grabbed my luggage, got off the car, and rushed out of this small town station.

It was three o'clock in the morning. In the shadows, several people surrounded me to grab my luggage, while shouting the names of some small inns. After my luggage was snatched by someone, I followed him to the second floor of an inn. He led me into a large room. In this room, there was a row of long bunks along one side, and two single wooden beds. A traveler who looked like a small businessman also seemed to have just arrived. I quickly washed my face and went downstairs to the accounting room to ask if the bus would run as usual tomorrow. The boss, smoking a water pipe, showed a professional smile and said:

"If it doesn't snow anymore, this little bit of snow won't be a problem."

But if it snows again, it's hard to say! So I worriedly kept pushing open the window to look at the snow. The snow was falling wildly, without any intention of stopping. Under the window was a rickshaw, and a mule standing in the snow was constantly ringing the small copper bell on its neck, making a kind of melancholic sound.

When I woke up in the morning, it was already bright. I quickly pushed open the window. The snow seemed to have stopped, but the sky was still the same. I turned around and ran downstairs, but I bumped into my roommate. He said:

"It's okay, the car can't run today, we're all on the same road."

I went back and briefly talked to him for a few words. Then I realized that he was a regular customer of this small inn, always running back and forth on this road. After talking for a while, he said:

"Let's go, let's get something to eat. How about Chaotian Restaurant? It would be a pity to come to Weixian and not eat Chaotian food!"

"What is Chaotian food?" I asked inexplicably.

"Try it and see? It's a specialty of Weixian."

So I followed him curiously and aimlessly. At this time, it started snowing again. In the muddy ground, the semi-circles trampled by mules were filled with pools of snow water.

Pulling open a greasy door, we stepped into a room with a strong oily smell. In the center of the room was a boiling pot, surrounded by a circle of red wooden pot stands, looking just like a big hot pot placed on a small round table. Because the weather was cold and it was still early, the room was deserted and there were no customers. Even the owner of the store ran out from the back room after we called out a few times. As soon as the boss came out, he grinned his greasy face and said:

"You came at the right time, the meat just came out of the pot!"

Following my friend's example, I sat down on the small lacquered stools scattered around the pot stand. The boss immediately put two bowls and two pairs of firewood-like chopsticks. Several wooden spoons were hanging on the edge of the pot. My friend picked up one and scooped the oily soup floating in the boiling pot of meat into his bowl, then scooped another spoonful and brought it close to his mouth, slowly sipping it twice, before putting down the spoon and saying:

"Give me a little bit of everything, I want the fatty kind, especially more fatty intestines."

After speaking, he turned to me and asked:

"What about you?"

"Give me some liver." I said casually.

The boss cut a portion, put it in a colander, and boiled it in the surging pot. Then he picked up a large, thick cake, rolled the meat in the cake, and handed it to my friend in a rough manner. I felt a strong interest and took my rolled cake. I sipped some soup and felt a little "unable to handle it", but the cake rolled with liver was good, very satisfying, and with the addition of green onions and pickles, it was even more flavorful, quite like the style of Liangshan heroes!

Page 18

While eating, I spit out a question from my mouth full of cake:

"Why is this called Chaotian Restaurant?"

The boss lifted his apron and wiped his greasy hands and replied:

"That's because in the early years, they were all opened on the street, with the pot mouth facing the sky. Now most of them are in the house."

My companion, chewing on a mouthful of cake, mumbled:

"It's also called offal pot, and some people also call it gluttonous pot, haha!"

A few crumbs of cake and spittle stars sprayed out with my companion's laughter.

After eating, I took a cup of dark red tea from the mud pot and poured it down in one breath, then I exhaled the onion smell and stepped onto the snowy street.

Old Clerk

— Shu Mang

The faint sunlight shone on the window glass of the silent office. In a stream of sunlight like water, countless dust particles could be seen moving. Everything seemed so dead and so gloomy. Stationery cabinets, desks, files, ledgers... Everything that constantly disturbed and frightened people's minds was neatly arranged, like coffins in a funeral home. In the midst of these things, people, for the sake of life, buried their energy, their youth, their hopes, and their laughter so plainly and silently...

Secretary Wang raised his head from a page of neat regular script documents, put down his pen, relaxed his old, sore, and somewhat numb arms. The heavy mind made him feel a kind of nausea close to his heart, and the only stream of sunlight flowing into the room from the window also pricked his eyes: in front of him seemed to be a pitch-black mass, but in this pitch-black mass there were chaotic, disturbing, and miscellaneous colors. He helplessly blinked his eyes, leaned back in his chair, and tightly held his hands together, his hands dripping with cold sweat.

"After all, as I get older, it's really not working..."

Indeed, Secretary Wang really felt himself getting older day by day. A man in his fifties, copying tens of thousands of words of neat regular script every day in a dark and sunless corner! That has been nineteen years! Nineteen years! What a long time! For the sake of his wife, children, and old mother, for the salary that never exceeded fifty yuan a month, he buried his past years for nineteen years! And now, the burden of life is still heavy, but he can only carefully keep this job. Nineteen years! Former colleagues, now, have relied on their "skills" and other people's "connections" to rise to high positions, but he, even after nineteen years, near the age of sixty, is still a "Secretary Wang" making fifty yuan a month, with no "skills" and no "connections". However, he is unable to support himself day by day, getting older day by day—in the past few months, superiors have successively discovered many mistakes in the documents he copied. He was called in by his superiors, who said in a mocking tone, "You are really too tired, at such an old age..."—but the burden of life is heavy.

Thinking of this, Secretary Wang felt a little moisture in his dry eyes, and he was miserable. A line of life's sorrow, like fierce liquor, pierced straight into his heart. He slightly opened his eyes, wiped them with a towel, took a breath, and picked up the cold and hard pen, dipped it in ink, and used the habit he had developed for nineteen years, carefully and cautiously, writing down one word at a time; "Check..."

In the quiet night, the door slammed open, and a messenger walked up to Secretary Wang and said in a low voice: "Mr. Wang, Section Chief Lu wants you to go right away."

Thinking for a moment, "Don't tell me I made a mistake somewhere again...?" Thinking so, he blankly put down his pen and followed the messenger out.

This time, Section Chief Lu seemed particularly polite: "Mr. Wang, you must be very tired... Yes, the work here is really too hard. Mr. Wang has been here for...?"

"Nineteen years, Section Chief."

"Yes, yes, nineteen years, even longer than my seniority, admirable, admirable, you should be called a veteran, shouldn't you? Hahahaha... How old is Mr. Wang this year...?"

"Fifty-eight."

"Yes, yes, for nineteen years, Mr. Wang has been working here, and the results have been very... We admire it, but I see that Mr. Wang is getting old, and excessive labor makes us very uneasy. We are thinking of Mr. Wang... so... so... here is... please take a look..."

He handed over an envelope. Secretary Wang took it and pulled it out to look: it was a letter of dismissal!

Suddenly startled, Secretary Wang was stunned. "What was coming has finally arrived." All sorts of complicated questions could no longer be thought about. Stumbling out of the gate, the sun on the street still shone brightly.

He calculated that he had not seen the sun on a Monday morning street for nineteen years...

People Who Failed in Life

— Tian Qi

In the living room of the inn, I accidentally met a distant relative who was in the business of green fruit canning in the town. In the past few years, every time I went home and passed through Songzhen, if I had time, I would go to his shop to see him and his wife. At that time, it was the peak of his "business boom". His nose was originally red and shiny, and people called him "Red Nose Duke". He was also good at talking. At that time, a kind of spirited and high-spirited demeanor was often revealed on his red and shiny nose. This unexpected meeting tonight, under the bright and dazzling gaslight, I took a brief look at him. He was wearing a set of old clothes and a tattered overcoat. That most noticeable red nose seemed to have faded away from its former spirited and shiny color, becoming rather shabby. He seemed very happy, calling out my name. I let him sit down in the room. After exchanging greetings, the two began to talk.

He began by complimenting me on my "glorious return", which made my face flush again and again. The conversation shifted to the situation of the market. At this time, he was almost the only one who spoke. He sighed, shook his head, and repeatedly said that business was getting worse every day. Without cash to pay, the goods from above could not be moved. Even with the goods, they could not be sold. Although there were more "foreign guests" than in previous years, they were all "wax ducks" with only enough money for transportation. The last time he settled the accounts, he couldn't pay, so he sold the only three acres of paddy fields in his family. Then he talked about a whole set of family disputes. He looked like he was about to cry.

At this time, he took a sip of tea and said in a low voice:

——I really didn't expect that my fortune would decline to this point! You don't know, it was earlier this year, I shouldn't have married that "Tiger Woman" behind the back of my wife. At that time, I said that there were also two or three acres of paddy fields in the family, and there should always be someone to manage and watch the house, but I didn't expect today...

It turned out that he had married a woman at home behind the back of his first wife. When his business failed and the fields were sold out, he couldn't afford to provide her with living expenses every month, forcing the woman to come to the store to make a scene. Now, all the money in and out of the store is controlled by the first wife. The woman couldn't stand it and went back home.

From beginning to end, I didn't say a word to him. I just felt that this was the inevitable fate of a ruined petty bourgeois. I sent him out at the foot of the stairs.

Early the next morning, I got up to prepare to take the bus to Kaixian County. When I rushed to the station, the bus was about to leave. Just as I took a seat, I turned around. Outside the bus window without glass, a head suddenly pushed in. He apologized and wanted me to say a word to him. In a secluded corner on the right side of the station, he timidly took out two large oranges from a large satchel and stuffed them into my hand. Then, with his left hand, he handed over a paper package and whispered into my ear:

—Here are fifty cents, please give them to her for me, and tell her for me...

Saying this, he turned his head, looked around, and said again:

—You are a well-read and enlightened person, please tell her for me: "If you want to leave, just leave. If you don't want to leave, it's up to you. But I can't afford to support you in the future. You can choose one of the two paths." Finally, he urged me to keep it a secret for him.

The horn sounded. I held the oranges in one hand and a package of silver coins in the other. Thinking of this man's failure, that woman's future, my heart felt like I had eaten something greasy, just feeling extremely stuffy.

The car was already bumping forward on the steep mountain road. (Miscellaneous Notes on the Return Journey)

The Road of Life

Hua Ruonan - Unwilling to be used by her father as a commodity for promotion and fortune, she left her family and fled to Shanghai alone. It is of course very difficult for a woman without money to live in Shanghai. She is unwilling to work in a factory and be teased by the foremen and small clerks, and she is unwilling to be a vase in a company or shop. She wants to be a female teacher but no one introduces her. She submits articles to various newspapers, but she doesn't know anyone in the literary world. In this helpless situation, she owes money to the rice store and two months' rent to the landlord.

Mr. Mi from the rice store came to collect the rice money. In the end, he had no choice but to return.

Miss Fang, the landlord's daughter, came to ask for the rent on behalf of her mother, saying that it must be paid today. Ruonan told her to wait for the money to be sent from home and she would give it to them immediately. Miss Fang would not allow it. Miss Fang also said, is it possible for a woman to have no way to make a living in Shanghai? As long as you are willing to be a little casual, isn't it easy to make some money? Ruonan was sad enough to hear this. She told her that she had already sold her soul and body twice in order to live... Her father received a report from Ruonan's cousin. He and her brother—Guoying—came here to ask her to go back! And marry that Commander Chen, but Ruonan refused to go back with her father! She resolutely refused to be Commander Chen's concubine and let her father use her as a commodity for promotion and fortune.

While the two sides were arguing, Ruonan's lover—Yifeng—came to find her from Hankou after receiving the information. Seeing this situation, he stopped her father and brother from taking Ruonan home. Suddenly—Ruonan said that she had been a slave woman and had sold her soul and body twice because of the pressure of life. Her father was so angry that he fainted and no longer wanted Ruonan to go back. The affection between father and daughter was gone at this time. Instead, the father scolded her and left with Guoying without looking back!

At this time, Ruonan completely realized that the reason her father wanted her was not because of the love between father and daughter, but completely because he wanted to use her as a commodity!…

Yifeng told Ruonan that we can only struggle and fight to live!

Cai Xiaofang's Mao Family Book

China-West (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening "Spring Boudoir Song"

Little peach blossoms cover the Shanglin Garden. The Su Causeway in the spring dawn, willows sway with gold. The color of the willows on the road is as green as can be. Rain hits the banana leaves, the doors are deeply closed. Butterflies in love fly as spring departs. Falling flowers and weather are of most concern. Deep in the boudoir hangs a beaded curtain. Birds startle and chirp, protecting the fallen petals. That Liu Niang was thrice drunk on Yang Guifei's couch. A dual-toned hatred for this unfaithful man. He and I, we first met at the Three Pools Mirroring the Moon. Long willow threads tie our hearts together. He loves me, the peacock spreads its screen with beautiful colors. I love him, riding a horse with a whip is a prince. We made a vow of mandarin ducks at West Lake. It's like, a pair of butterflies flying back and forth frequently. At times, peach and plum blossoms compete for spring, leaving beautiful shadows. At times, we recite poems in old age, advising literary pursuits. Who knew, that the drunken old man's attempt to catch the moon would be an empty hope. Hating that the Eastern Emperor's four seasons are not constant spring. A sudden thunderbolt on a clear day. It's just like, swords rising in the east. He is defending the nation and the people, traveling to Shanghai. Suddenly singing the Yangguan Three Stanzas. Thrice drunk before the wine cup, bidding farewell at the long pavilion. I wish him, to return early with the dragon boat race victory. Double phoenixes facing the sun, drunk in peace. We are happy and enjoying peace and prosperity. Who knows, that spring returns to the small garden, but he has not returned. The wild goose falls on the sandy beach, with little news. How can a patterned brocade be delivered? The parasitic plant's traces have no roots. Now the round fan weeps in the autumn wind. It's more miserable than Zhao Jun's resentment. The candle shadow sways red in loneliness. The sound of waves and the shadows of plum blossoms sigh in drifting. The hate is deeper than the Qu River of Xiao and Xiang.

Xu Wenbi's Opening

Aviation (1180) 11:15 AM to 12:00 PM

Opening "Receiving Vomit"

The jade beauty's singing and dancing have not yet returned. Lonely Qin Tower, cold emerald terrace. The precious mirror has not been put away, the curtain is raised. Listening to the sound of the night watchman's clapper and drum. Lazily. Intent lingering. Glad to see the courtesan returning drunk. Her cheeks are flushed with wine. Helplessly, the jade sleeves droop down. The procuress supports her, delicate and weak. Beauty hides her shame, unwilling to raise her head. The procuress happily claims there are guests. The beauty is drunk and cannot accompany. On the bed, her starry eyes are blurred and sleepy. Qin Zhong is. A long night accompanies the fragrance. Immediately takes a towel to personally receive the vomit. Calls for tea and humbly offers a cup of dew. The golden rooster awakens her from a dream of immortals. Asking, who is this gentleman. Little maiden. My name is Qin Zhong, selling oil. Last spring I saw you and admired your talent. Accumulating money for a good meeting. Last night I chanced upon you returning drunk. Respectfully receiving your vomit. Quickly taking clothes to accompany you. The beauty listened and said it was rare. Thanking you for your kindness and apologizing for the trouble. Qin Zhong is indeed sincere and serious. Thank you for your kindness and talent. Cautiously asking when we will meet again.

Gao Mangsheng, who went to Nanjing with the Shanghai Opera Society, has now joined the Mingyue Society and is serving as the backstage director in Jincheng, and plans to go to Qingdao, North China after the Jincheng period expires. (Monila)

Movie News

Pan Yuzhen Returns Home with Praise, Performing at Carlton Starting Wednesday

The Pan Yuzhen Art Troupe, which once performed at the Shanghai Nanjing Grand Theater, was ordered by the government to go abroad to participate in the Chicago World's Fair competition before the year, and was greatly praised by the people there. They continued to perform at Broadway in New York and other places, breaking any record of Chinese opera troupes in the United States. This art troupe, with Yuzhen, Yujie, Yurong, and Yulan as the pillars, also has a warrior Su Fu and more than twenty other actors, each with unique skills and performing very seriously, so their reputation can shake overseas. They have now returned to China, and it is rumored that they will perform at the Carlton Theater starting on Wednesday, and it is expected to cause another sensation. In order to particularly please the audience, the theater will also show the martial arts epic "Hero on Horseback" at the same time.

"Peaches and Plums Compete for Beauty" Lead Actress Ye Qiuxin

— Ma Yonghua Photo

Silver Scribbles

— Zhi Er

Female stars opening silk shops and crowning dance queens, this was popular two or three years ago. It seems like without doing this, it was impossible to increase their "reputation." Following this, it was probably "when things reach their peak, they decline," and most female stars were ashamed to participate in these boring activities. Therefore, people said that this was the female stars' awakening, a commendable phenomenon.

Is it the female stars' awakening? What is the explanation for the recent Gu Meijun and Gu Lanjun participating in the opening of silk shops, and Yuan Meiyun crowning the "Queen of Flowers"?

Wang Tingshu, who played the clown in the Lion Roar Society's "Death of a Famous Actor," received good reviews for a while. It is said that this gentleman did indeed play a clown in the North before, so it is no wonder that he played it so well.

Also, it is reported that the clown gentleman has joined the Shanghai Theater Academy with Chen Ningqiu, and there are four others who have joined together. It seems that the Lion Roar Society is likely to merge with and be under the command of the "theater senior" Xiang Peiliang.

Chen Ningqiu once told people that his joining the Shanghai Theater was like entering a big hotel, at least he wouldn't have to worry about food and lodging in the future.

Someone invited Wei Ling to join the Shanghai Theater, but Wei is still considering it.

Shao Zuiweng came to Shanghai reportedly wanting to "wholesale" some dancers to Nanyang, has the Cantonese sound film failed again? But after the "wholesale" of dancers fails again, what "business" will Boss Shao do?

Small Records of Lianhua Filmmakers

Yin Xiucen used to be a small factory owner, he knew how to make guns and artillery, but he didn't know how to make bullets.

Cinematographer Huang Shaofen used to be an actor. In "Love and Duty," he played the brother of Chen Yan Yan, who had the same mother but not the same father.

Ma Xuweibang is a painter. For a period of time, he relied on painting for a living.

Zhang Weitian, who writes subtitles, has been in the Chinese film industry for almost twenty years, but he has never been on camera once. According to him: "If I stand in front of the camera, I get dizzy as if someone is pointing a gun at me."

Wu Yonggang, the director of "Waves Washing Sand," and Xu Ke, the set designer of the film, were classmates at the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts.

Before entering the film industry, Liu Jiqun was a student at Soochow University in Suzhou.
